New Office of the Northern Station of the Two-Roads Administration Held Groundbreaking Ceremony Yesterday, Ten-Story Building Costs 700,000 Yuan, Invested and Built by the Roads Savings Association 104

The office of the Jinghu-Huhangyong Roads Administration was destroyed in the January 28th Incident. Although it was repaired, it was still insufficient for use. Nearby houses were rented to serve as offices, but the rent burden was heavy, and it was inconvenient to contact business when various departments were scattered. Therefore, with the consent of the Administration's Endowment Reserve Fund Management Committee and the approval of the Ministry of Railways, 700,000 yuan was invested to build a ten-story building in the North Station. The design had already been finalized, and construction was started. Yesterday at 2:00 PM, a groundbreaking ceremony was held. The ceremony was very simple. In addition to the director, deputy director, and department heads of the Administration, Davison, the representative of the China-British Bank Corporation, Pu Dengqing, the representative of the Endowment Reserve Fund Management Committee, Chen Chengshi, the representative of the Two-Roads Party Department, Zhao Jue, the representative of the Two-Roads Labor Union, and more than 100 others attended. Director Huang presided over the ceremony and reported. After a speech by the representative of the China-British Bank Corporation, the groundbreaking ceremony was held. The events are recorded below.

Meeting Place Set Up in North Station

The office building of the Administration is located on the east side of the North Station. The foundation engineering has been completed, and wooden frames are being built to carry out the construction on the ground. Yesterday, a thatched shed was specially built at the main entrance of the building for the groundbreaking ceremony. The cornerstone was covered with the national flag, and the stone surface was engraved with the words "The Office of the Jinghu-Huhangyong Roads Administration was destroyed in the January 28th Incident in the 21st year of the Republic of China, and the groundbreaking ceremony for reconstruction was held on March 7th in the 25th year of the Republic of China, Director Huang Boqiao, Deputy Director Wu Shaozeng, Recorded by Shen Enfu." The meeting place was set up in the conference room on the second floor of the North Station. The party and national flags were hung at the station entrance, and many road police were dispatched to be stationed there. At 2:00 PM, the representatives arrived at the meeting and the ceremony began.

(Photo by Lie)

Director Huang's Report

After the formalities, Chairman and Director Huang delivered a speech, saying that after the office of the Two Roads Administration was destroyed in the January 28th Incident in the 21st year of the Republic of China, it was unavoidable to borrow four offices in the public concession. However, the rent was extremely expensive, so the situation of each department being cramped was unbearable, and when there were places that should be contacted, it was inconvenient to travel back and forth. Then, each department gradually concentrated near the North Station, and the office space was divided into six places, but the annual rental expenses were nearly 70,000 yuan. If the house was rented for ten years, 700,000 yuan would be spent. Therefore, when each office moved, it planned to build its own office, but only because it did not have the financial resources for a while, it first built the vehicle department and the Shangbei Station office building at the site of the Administration's old office for more than 50,000 yuan. On the one hand, it negotiated with the Timber Road Endowment Reserve Management Committee to fund the construction of a suitable office building and sell it to the Administration. Fortunately, the members of the Endowment Committee enthusiastically supported it, and the Ministry of Railways approved it and decided to build a building worth 700,000 yuan and auxiliary houses with various electrical, sanitary, and heating equipment, and sell it to the Administration for use. The Administration will pay the money in installments within ten years. The Administration and the Endowment Committee have a contract with the following important clauses: 1. The office building is set as a formal six floors, plus a canteen, electrical equipment, water tank, and machine room, with a smaller four floors, for a total of ten floors. The location of its auxiliary houses will be notified to the Endowment Committee in writing by the Road Administration and attached to this contract as an attachment. 2. The sale price of the aforementioned buildings, together with interest, shall be amortized by the Road Administration in the form of monthly rent, with a maximum period of ten years, but the Road Administration may pay it off in one lump sum at any time. 3. The investment interest of the aforementioned buildings shall be calculated at an annual rate of six percent during the construction period, and at an annual rate of seven percent when the road administration moves in when the houses are completed. 4. The repayment of principal and interest shall commence in the month when the houses are officially completed and the Road Administration moves in to work. 5. The interest on the construction funds shall be calculated from the date of each payment to ensure fairness. The interest that is not due at the time of repayment of the principal shall be settled in one lump sum when the houses are completed and the Road Administration moves in, and shall be included as the principal of the construction funds. 6. Before the principal and interest of the construction funds are paid off, the aforementioned buildings shall still be owned by the Endowment Committee. 7. All taxes, insurance premiums, and regular repair fees for the office buildings and auxiliary houses shall be borne by the Road Administration. It should also be reported here that the Endowment Committee has funded the construction of the police fourth section office of the Xihu section on the early bridge. The bidding has been started for construction. This house is the auxiliary house in the contract, and the expenses are also paid within the 700,000 yuan. Moreover, with the efforts of all parties, the total completion in the future may be less than 700,000 yuan, and after ten years, the Administration will get a building and auxiliary houses, which is more cost-effective than renting houses in the concession and paying large rents every year without getting anything in the end. Compared to the Two Roads Administration, this investment is the safest and has no unexpected losses. Therefore, this move can be said to be in the interests of both parties, but I still represent the Administration to express my gratitude to the members, directors, consultants, and architects of the Endowment Committee. After the completion of the new office, the spirit of the colleagues will also be renewed, and today's groundbreaking ceremony is a commemorative ceremony for the beginning of a new life for the colleagues of the Administration. I have endless hope.

Speeches by Two Representatives

Then, Davison, the representative of the China-British Bank Corporation, gave a speech, saying that he was very honored to participate in the ceremony, but he was not prepared to speak, so he had no opinions to express, but he expressed his congratulations on the new construction of the Road Administration and wished the road affairs would become more and more developed. It was decided that Pu Dengqing, the representative of the Endowment Reserve Fund Management Committee, would give a speech, saying that the Two Roads Endowment Reserve Fund Association has been established for more than ten years, and the stored funds have reached millions of yuan. It has always stored funds in banks and purchased public bonds and stocks, etc., as safe investments. Now that the Road Administration is building its own building and lacks cash, it has agreed to invest 700,000 yuan to engage in construction. The society has obtained a safe investment, and the Road Administration can also obtain a dog building after ten years, which is a win-win situation. After the speech, the groundbreaking ceremony was held in front of the new building. Director Huang put the commemorative copper box under the cornerstone, added cement to solidify the seal, and then announced the completion of the ceremony, took photos, and dispersed.

Director Huang Holds Groundbreaking Ceremony (Photo by International News Agency)

New Office Engineering

The middle part of the new office is ten stories high (including water tank and machine room), and the two wings are six stories high. The length is 233 feet deep, the two wings are 55 feet each, and the middle part is 56 feet. The height of the two wings is 77 feet, and the middle part is 112 feet. The total area is 8,500 square meters. The construction project is contracted by Xu Shunxing Construction Factory for 349,800 yuan in national currency. The internal electrical equipment is contracted by Rosen De Foreign Company for 26,949 yuan in national currency. The telephone equipment is contracted by Siemens Electric Factory for 33,040 yuan in national currency. The elevator equipment is contracted by Jardine Matheson Machinery Company for 17,800 yuan in national currency and 43,966 francs in Swiss currency. The heating and sanitary equipment is contracted by Xin Shen Sanitary Engineering Company for 58,680 yuan in national currency. The vault door equipment is contracted by Hezhong Company for 3,355 US dollars. The rooftop water tower can hold 15,000 gallons. It is planned to build a deep water well to facilitate fire protection, and the machine room can control the electrical equipment of the entire station.

This City's Women's Association to Commemorate "March 8th" Today; Rural Area Propaganda and Guan Bo Speech; Jointly Held by Seven Women's Organizations 105

Today is International Women's Day. To awaken rural women from their state of ignorance, this city's Women's Association, with all its directors, will personally set out to various places with obstructed transportation and backward education to conduct extensive and universal propaganda. They have also invited Mayor Wu's wife, Mrs. Cai Yuanpei, Ms. Shu Huizhen, and others to broadcast the significance of March 8th and to issue "A Declaration to Women on International Women's Day" on the Greater China Asia Sound Radio Station. The original text is recorded below: "Dear sisters, 'March 8th' is a day for international women to jointly seek their own liberation. Therefore, until the women's masses have achieved complete liberation, it should have great commemorative significance. Although women in Western countries have obtained many rights and opportunities equal to men on the surface since the 19th century, the consequences of the World War have ultimately led to misfortune, which has intensified. Therefore, after the European War, all countries, both economically and socially, have fallen into extreme panic and chaos. Imperialists, in order to make up for their losses in the war and restore their dreamed-of inherent prosperity, have had to intensify their oppression and exploitation of women. At the same time, because of the extreme preparation for the second great massacre, they have had to use the pretext of 'preserving the race' to drive women to exhaust themselves in production and supply new materials for the battlefield. Today, women have become one of the targets of the world's reactionary trends. To escape trampling and not become victims of the countercurrent, we can only continue the spirit of March 8th and strive forward. As for our country, gender equality, although clearly stated in the party program and recorded in the laws, when examining the reality, the so-called political and legal equality is nothing more than a blank sheet of paper, and the so-called social and economic equality is even more of an elusive illusion. The same moral law does not apply to both men and women, and the scope of women's occupations is shrinking day by day. All these facts prove that the liberation of Chinese women is still far away, and the nominal equality between men and women is due to this. Unless we are content with the status quo and willingly be the former slaves of men, we should follow in the footsteps of the fighting paths of our predecessors and strive bravely forward. Since 'September 18th' to this day, China has been fragmented, the countryside has gone bankrupt, and internal and external troubles have become increasingly serious. In other words, the fate of the Chinese nation is on the verge of survival. Women cannot exist independently of the nation, nor can they seek their own solutions independently of the issue of national survival. Therefore, Chinese women, in addition to fighting for their own liberation, should also strive for national liberation. 'March 8th' is a day for international women to jointly seek liberation. In the eyes of women who have already been liberated, it is good news, and their formal commemoration is naturally a celebration. However, in the eyes of Chinese women under internal and external troubles, it can only be a warning sign, and the expression that comes with this warning sign is the spirit of going to war and the determination to resist. Sisters, rise up together, unite closely, continue the spirit of the fighting of the enlightened, shoulder the unfinished mission of our predecessors, and promote women's liberation, human equality, and world peace."

Furthermore, seven organizations, including the China Women's Movement League, the China Women's Temperance Association, the Shanghai Young Women's Christian Association, the China Women's Society, the Chinese Women's Association, the Bee Society, and the Shanghai Women's National Salvation Association, have scheduled a joint commemorative conference at the Sichuan Road YMCA at 2:00 PM today. Ms. Wang Canzhi, He Xiangning, Wang Xiaoying, Shi Liang, Liu Wang Liming, Lei Sai, and other prominent women figures will give speeches. The presidium consists of seven people: Chen Lingyi, Wang Ruizhu, Zhang Manyun, Bu Zhenhua, Xie Zuyi, Shi Liang, and Zhang Zhixue. Staff members from each organization will be assigned to serve as receptionists, security, recorders, masters of ceremonies, and other duties. Women from all walks of life are welcome to attend.

Market Stability, Business Activity; Various Banks Sequentially Return Loans; Bank of China Implements Interbank Collateral Lending; Promotes Bills and Expands Rural Lending 107

After the implementation of the new currency system policy, the market is stable and various industries are active. The Bank of China's adjustment of interbank collateral lending has been implemented, and money shops have been sequentially returning loans to the three banks. Efforts are being made to promote acceptance bills, and various banks and shops are making every effort to expand rural lending. The details are recorded as follows:

Organizing Collateral Loans for Various Shops

The Bank of China, in order to regulate interbank finance and organize collateral loans for various shops, has implemented the measures after consultation between the bank's general manager, Song Hanzhang, and money industry leaders Qin Runqing, He Zhongxiao, and others. Any money shop can mortgage valuable goods and bonds to the bank for cash at about 70% of the market price, with a particularly low monthly interest rate. Generally, each shop is limited to 200,000 national currency. Those with receipts and payments of more than 10 million yuan can obtain the bank's consent for a limit of 500,000 national currency, indirectly providing relief to industry and commerce.

Money Shops Return Loans

The Ministry of Finance allocated 25 million yuan in financial public bonds last year to rescue the money industry, and a Money Industry Supervision Committee was established to manage it. In addition to the 7 million yuan from various commercial banks and the money industry reserve, which has already been repaid, the 18 million yuan from the three banks of China, Central, and Communications, with the permission of the Ministry of Finance and the three banks, has been extended to the end of the Republic of China year 24 before being returned. Now, the various money shops that borrowed the money, since using legal tender, have increased their chips, and various industries have gradually become active. Therefore, they have been sequentially returning the loans from the three banks.

Promoting Bill Acceptance

The member banks and money shops of the Banking and Money Industry Association, in view of the decline in the market last year and the difficulty in lending, have been forced to tighten up this year and be particularly cautious about various loans. Now, since the implementation of the new currency system policy, the market has seen an increase in chips, and the industry itself has been consolidated. In order to implement the relief of industry and commerce, they are planning to establish a bank and money shop bill acceptance center, promote acceptance bills, and study reducing deposit and loan interest rates to promote industrial and commercial prosperity.

Expanding Rural Lending

Various banks, in view of the urgent task of revitalizing the countryside, the China Agricultural Loan Banking Group, jointly established by the Shanghai, Communications, Zhejiang Xingye, and Xinhua banks, has decided to solicit cooperation from various banks and money shops this year and make every effort to expand. At the same time, the Agricultural Bank of China has received 50 million yuan from the Ministry of Finance to handle rural land lending, and General Manager Xu has drafted detailed measures, which were approved for implementation at yesterday's board meeting. In addition, the Bank of China is also making every effort to expand rural lending.

Zhabei Lumber Merchants Went on Strike Yesterday Morning; Protesting Tax Increases and Arbitrary Arrests; Sent Representatives to Party and Government Agencies to Petition 108

—City Chamber of Commerce Sent Letter Urging Prompt Resumption of Business—

The lumber merchants on Guangfu Road in Zhabei all rent land to build houses. According to usual practice, the property tax is 14% of the assessed value. In the autumn of the Republic of China year 23, the collection office re-evaluated the value, resulting in a tax increase of more than double. In the summer of year 24, it was increased by another one to two times. This spring, it was increased by another one to several times. It was also stipulated that the property tax for years 23 and 24 must be paid according to the new tax amount for year 25. If less was paid in years 23 and 24, a fine of 20% will be imposed. The lumber merchants, with the property tax increasing repeatedly, reaching six or seven times the original amount, have repeatedly objected, but all efforts have been ineffective, resulting in the issue remaining unresolved.

Arbitrary Arrests

Public Indignation

On the 3rd of this month, the lumber merchants on Guangfu Road petitioned the Finance Bureau, stating that they could only pay the tax amount for year 24 at most, and firmly opposed the new measures and penalty regulations for year 25, but received no reply. At 12:00 noon that day, the collection office sent personnel to Fu Tai to collect taxes. Still unable to reach an agreement on the new and old tax amounts, the tax collector took the manager of that company, Chen Hongzhang, to the collection office for a meeting, ordering him to pay in full. When he was unable to comply, he was detained at the Menggu Road Police Station at 6:00 PM. At noon on the 4th, he was transferred to the North Railway Station Branch, and at 1:00 PM, he was transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. He was photographed and fingerprinted. Only after the public office and the trade association intervened and guaranteed his release, was he released, still limited to paying the money within three days. The merchants, because this matter had not been decided by the court and the arbitrary arrest procedures had been delayed, decided to go on strike in response.

Yesterday Morning, Industry Issued Strike Notice

At 9:00 AM yesterday morning, more than a dozen lumber companies on Guangfu Road, including Yuan Xing at No. 76, Fu Ji at No. 62, Xie Sheng at No. 755, Heng Xiang at No. 999, Fu [blank] at No. 1047, Rui Da at No. [blank] 77, Da Chang at No. 1059, Zi Da at No. 1073, Yuan Shun at No. 1105, Yong Da at No. 691, Da Feng, Xiang Mao, and Xie Mao, all declared a strike. A notice was posted on the door stating, "Due to the detention of Chen Hongzhang, manager of Fu Tai Lumber Company, by the Municipal North Collection Office, the industry is indignant and has voluntarily suspended business to await the decision on the petition."

Sent Representatives to Party and Government to Petition

At 10:00 AM yesterday morning, more than a dozen managers from various companies, including Zhang Yunrui, Lu Bingkun, Qu Jisheng, Shen Jingtang, and Chen Mingyuan, accompanied by Wei Shanfu, a representative from the public association, and Xu Zuoliang, a representative from the public office, went to the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the Municipal Government to petition. Their petition stated, (omitted above) "Now, according to letters from our colleagues Rui Da, Xie Sheng, Yuan Gu, Yuan Yu, Heng Xiang, Zi Da, Fu Ji, Da Chang, Xie Mao, Fu Tai, and other lumber companies, we respectfully state that our lumber industry has been affected by the economic downturn, and business is declining. All expenses have already been reduced with difficulty. How can we bear the burden of a sudden and huge increase in property tax? After investigation, the property tax of the industry was thoroughly investigated in year 22, with no omissions. The industry complied and paid the tax. In year 23, the tax was generally increased to one or more times, which was already a heavy burden. We endured and reluctantly complied, not daring to disobey. However, in the autumn of year 24, it was suddenly increased by one or several times, and the industry is indeed facing the situation of heavy taxes and unbearable burdens. We requested your association to convey our difficulties to the Municipal Finance Bureau again and again, but it was not approved. We are still continuing to request. Unexpectedly, at 11:00 AM on the 3rd of this month, the Municipal North Collection Office led the police to arrest Chen Hongzhang, the manager of Fu Tai Lumber Company, without distinguishing right from wrong, and immediately detained him. At 6:00 PM, he was sent to the Second Precinct of the Fourth District and transferred to the Public Security Bureau. It was not until 4:00 PM on the afternoon of the decision that your association, together with Yuan Shun, Heng Xiang, Rui Da, Xie Sheng, Fu Ji, Zi Da, Da Chang, and Xie Mao lumber companies, bailed him out and ordered him to pay within three days. According to Article 16, Paragraph 1, the last paragraph of the Shanghai Municipal Property Tax Regulations revised in [Year] 24, the regulations for resisting tax are only to summon the case for collection, not to summon the case for detention. The so-called collection has legitimate collection procedures, and illegal detention cannot be abused without legitimate procedures. The laws of the State and the National Government state that the personal freedom of the people must not be arbitrarily arrested, and the violation of the law is undeniable. Let us put this aside and not discuss the individual's right to sue. Now, let us examine Article 5 of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau's Investigation of Rent Method, which stipulates that the maximum amount of tax to be recovered is one year's tax amount. Now, even according to its unilaterally determined highest limit of 333 yuan and 91 cents for one year's tax amount, the amount to be recovered is 407 yuan and 68 cents, plus a fine of 81 yuan and 54 cents, which is indeed a violation of the regulations. Furthermore, after investigating our colleagues' houses, some of them are self-built, and the property tax should be assessed accordingly. The lumber yard should also be assessed. The assessment was decided twice in years 22 and 23. Even if the previous investigation and assessment were not accurate, they should be submitted to the Housing Evaluation Committee for evaluation in accordance with the regulations. However, without an explicit evaluation, the tax was suddenly increased several times based solely on the investigator's report, which is inevitably arbitrary. Recently, our colleagues have received notices from the collection office to increase the tax amount, and the amount to be supplemented generally exceeds the limit of one year. Due to the sluggish business, we are unable to bear the additional burden. Now, seeing Chen Hongzhang, a legitimate businessman, inevitably suffering oppression, we are all indignant and have voluntarily suspended business. We are specially appealing to your association, requesting immediate relief, negotiating legally, reducing excessive taxes, and correcting the punishment. We are extremely grateful." Based on this, the Shanghai Municipal Property Tax was investigated and estimated twice in years 22 and 23, and there are few omissions, which is true. The arrest of the manager of Fu Tai Lumber Company this time has made our colleagues wary of the collection of taxes, which is regrettable. However, in recent years, the market has declined, and our colleagues are indeed in a difficult situation to maintain. If we supervise and责责 excessively, it is not a way to relieve business difficulties. Now, the industry in that area has unanimously suspended business, and the industry throughout the city is indignant upon hearing of the previous situation, and there is an indication that they will suspend business together. Our association is deeply concerned that the situation will expand and affect the commercial and social order of this city. We believe that the situation is urgent and needs to be resolved quickly. Therefore, we are sending personnel to accompany representatives from the lumber companies to present this letter in person. We should ask for your assistance in dealing with the matter.

The Party Department Orders Immediate Resumption of Business

The Municipal Party Department of this city yesterday ordered the Shanghai Lumber Industry Association, "Regarding the illegal arrest and pursuit of property tax by the Municipal North Collection Office and the abuse of detention, the industry in that area has unanimously suspended business, and we earnestly request that you investigate and handle the matter legally. We order you to instruct the various merchants in the industry to resume business and await legal investigation and handling. This order is issued by Wu Xingya, Pan Gongzhan, and Tong Hangbai, members of the Standing Committee."

The Chamber of Commerce Advises the Association to Resume Business

The representatives first went to the Municipal Party Department to request (1) a temporary suspension of execution, (2) a re-evaluation of the tax amount, and (3) a guarantee that the same situation will not occur in the future. Zhu Yangwu of the Civil Movement Section met with them and advised the representatives to resume business first and await legal resolution. They then went to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, where Yuan Hongjun, a clerk of the Commerce Section, met with them and advised them to resume business first. He then accompanied them to the Municipal Government, where Cen Zixin, a staff member of the Second Section, met with them and replied that he would telegraph the Public Security Bureau to temporarily suspend execution before a resolution was reached. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce also sent a letter to the Lumber Association authorizing the members to resume business. The original text stated, "We respectfully state that regarding the strike of the industry due to the re-evaluation of property tax, this association has led representatives of the public association to the Shanghai Municipal Government to petition, and the Municipal Government has agreed to investigate and handle the matter and notified the Public Security Bureau to handle the matter of demanding payment within a limited time with leniency. In addition to presenting the dispute over rent evaluation to the Municipal Government, it should be evaluated by the Housing Evaluation Committee to show fairness and thoroughly investigate the illegal actions of the collection office. On the one hand, we should advise the members in Zhabei to resume business as usual and await resolution. This is our sincere hope."

After the Implementation of the New Telephone Regulations, All Sectors are Taking Countermeasures; Letters Request Various Industries to Calculate Losses; Jointly Use the Basic Fee; Willing to Dismantle and Hire Workers to Relay 112

The Application Society stated that the Special Zone Telephone Problem Committee sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, asking it to instruct the various industry associations to calculate the losses suffered by the telephone service this month in order to provide a basis for negotiations, and scheduled the fourth regular meeting on the 10th of this month to discuss further protest measures. The details are recorded below:

Statistics of Losses

The Telephone Problem Committee sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating, "Respectfully, since the implementation of the Shanghai Telephone Company's new charging regulations, the losses suffered by citizens have been quite large. In the autumn of commercial depression and social and economic collapse, the company only considers its own interests and does everything possible to exploit, which is hateful. Your association has repeatedly protested against this issue, and although it has failed to achieve the desired goal, it can also express the public's concerns. Now that the company's new regulations have been implemented, the losses suffered by the citizens should be clearly calculated in order to provide a basis for petitioning the government to take it back and run it independently. Your association is the general organization for all Shanghai businesses and strives to relieve the suffering of businessmen. Therefore, we specially request that you instruct the various industry associations to register the number of telephone fees paid starting in March and submit them to our association by April 10th. This matter concerns public welfare, and we hope you will investigate and handle it accordingly."

Saving Method

Committee member Zheng AoKui suggested a method to save telephone charges for traffic relief, stating, "Respectfully, each telephone set must bear a basic telephone charge, as much as 5 yuan and 5 jiao for stores and 3 yuan and 5 jiao for residences. If there are ten telephone sets in a certain lane, removing nine sets and reducing the installation to one set can save 35 yuan and 1 jiao in basic fees. Reducing the installation to one set for ten stores can save even more, 49 yuan and 5 jiao in basic fees. With this expense, specially hiring telephone operators will be more than sufficient, and even if each call costs three cents, it can be saved without exception. Compared to sacrificing to the telephone company for no reason, it is still a method in a situation where there is no method," etc. After receiving the letter, it is heard that the association will forward the letter to notify users to uniformly follow the method.

Willing to Dismantle

Telephone is a public utility, which has a great impact on the prosperity of commerce. The municipal authorities should consider how to promote the development of commerce in order to coexist and prosper. Now, the Public Works Department ignores the economic downturn and rashly allows the Shanghai Telephone Company to implement the new regulations, collecting charges according to the number of calls and increasing the burden on citizens in order to satisfy its monopolistic ambition and fulfill its desires. Now, the members of this association are willing to dismantle them all in order to adopt effective methods and actively resist, and to serve as a backing for your association. Because such expensive telephone charges, calculated at 20 calls per day, cost about 8 jiao, which amounts to more than 20 yuan per month. It is better to hire manual relay to save money, which can not only relieve unemployment but also resist it. We hereby submit this suggestion and hope that you will adopt it.

Lu Bohong Returns to Shanghai to Report on the Shandong Disaster; Proposes Three Relief Measures 115

The China and Foreign Relief Society on Renji Road believes that although the Shandong flood disaster has carried out emergency winter relief, the situation in the spring is still severe. The society has requested Director Lu Bohong to go to investigate and determine the spring relief policy. According to his return report, the disaster area in Shandong Province occupies a thousand square miles. Taking only a part of agricultural production, the losses are 26 million yuan. So far, the accumulated water is one or two feet deep, and boats cannot travel, making progress more difficult than before. At least three months of work is needed to solve the problem of closing the mouth of the breach. The original shelters have been maintained for seven months. Due to insufficient funds, in addition to returning the remaining people, there are still 300,000 people who are extremely destitute, and no less than 500,000 people remain in the flooded area. All the accumulated food and all those who can find a way to survive have been exhausted. The seven temporary hospitals established in the disaster area require 5,000 yuan per month to provide relief to sick refugees. The doctors, nurses, and others are all male and female missionaries volunteering, etc. Three relief measures are proposed as follows: Spring relief should be divided into emergency relief and agricultural relief. First, provide relief to the counties with the most severe disasters, and emergency relief should be limited to those who are extremely poor and unable to live. Agricultural relief should focus on the spring plowing problem in the disaster area, such as agricultural tools and seeds. Fundraising should be done in cooperation with the mountain government and various charitable organizations. Since the shelters have not yet been closed and the disaster area has not yet recovered, the hospitals should continue to operate for another two months until the end of May. It is proposed to provide loans to cooperative societies and to use work as relief for the victims, such as the Juye Chenggong and Zhukou Xiangong projects, etc., which are all suitable for work relief methods. It is heard that the association has scheduled a board meeting on the 10th of this month to discuss everything.

This City Will Report Smokers: Forced Registration of Smokers; License Renewal Begins April 1st; All Staff in Government and Organizations Must Be Cleared by a Deadline 116

Since the Municipal Public Security Bureau has been rigorously promoting anti-smoking efforts in this city, the number of smokers has gradually decreased. Regarding registered smokers, formal licenses will be renewed starting April 1st. As for the procedures for reporting smokers in this city, they will be implemented as soon as the anti-smoking headquarters issues the regulations to Shanghai. Details are as follows:

License Renewal to Start on April 1st

Smokers in this city were originally required to renew their licenses every six months. Licenses obtained during the voluntary registration period were valid from September 1st, 1935, to the end of February 1936. Licenses obtained during the mandatory registration period were valid from October 1st, 1935, to the end of March. However, many smokers have been negligent during the renewal period, resulting in inconsistencies. Therefore, to ensure strict enforcement, all licenses, whether obtained voluntarily or mandatorily, will be renewed starting April 1st. Notices will be posted in various districts on the date of the announcement to inform the public.

Smoker Reporting; Orders Not Yet Received

To ensure smokers quit within a specified period, the anti-smoking headquarters convened the first standing committee meeting of the anti-smoking association to discuss practical solutions. Fourteen articles on methods for reporting smokers were specifically drafted and circulated to all provinces and cities for implementation. Yesterday morning, a reporter from the Dagong News Agency visited Dai, the section chief of the Fourth Anti-Smoking Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, to inquire about the progress of implementing smoker reporting in this city. According to the response, although the anti-smoking headquarters has established regulations on reporting smokers, the official documents and methods have not yet been received. The bureau will implement them as soon as the regulations are issued.

Government Employees; Clearance by Deadline

Since the Municipal Public Security Bureau implemented anti-smoking efforts in this city, in addition to conducting voluntary and mandatory registration procedures for all smokers, all personnel in government agencies who are addicted to smoking, as well as staff in public organizations, will be strictly cleared after the reporting methods are announced. Those who conceal their addiction will be dismissed from their positions and punished according to the law if discovered.

National Photography Exhibition Preparatory Committee; Passed Regulations on Submissions and Other Matters 117

Photography is a new cultural tool, but our country lacks concrete promotion. Luo Gusun, president of the International News Photography Society, recognizing this, invited photography experts from across the country to initiate a National Photography Exhibition to promote the art. This has been reported previously. The committee held its second preparatory meeting in Shanghai yesterday and passed important proposals such as the organizational law of the preparatory committee, methods for raising exhibition funds, and regulations on exhibition submissions. They also planned to publish a special issue of the conference and compile the "Chinese Photography Yearbook of 1936." The exhibition date has been set for mid-April of this year, with exhibitions to be held in Nanjing and Shanghai first, followed by a tour of various provinces. It is sure to be a lively affair. The regulations for photography submissions are listed below: Regulations for the First National Photography Exhibition. This association is launching the National Photography Exhibition to assist education, promote culture, and enhance photographic art. The qualifications of exhibitors are listed as follows: A. Individuals who love photography; B. Professional photographers; C. Photography groups. The scope of submissions: A (Subjects): Art; News; Nature (natural landscapes and scenic spots, as well as flora and fauna); Science (sound, light, chemistry, electricity, aviation, underwater, mechanics, astronomy, medicine, etc.); Architecture; Production and Construction; Life; Advertising; Decoration. B (Quantity): No more than twelve pieces for a systematic series; no more than ten individual pieces per person. C (Types): Monochrome; Natural Color; Slides. D (Sizes): Art photography is limited to 12 inches; other categories are from 6 to 12 inches. If there are special circumstances, the length and width dimensions are not counted. All submissions must not be mounted on cardboard. Mounting procedures will be handled by the association. Submissions must include the exhibitor's name, category, title, name, and address on the submission form and on the back of the submission. If self-photographed, please also attach a sample print of each type, size is not restricted. Except for art photography, which must be personally taken, all other categories, obtained through usual collection, are acceptable for submission. The submissions will be reviewed by a review committee specially organized by the association. Experts will be hired to evaluate and award prizes after the close of the exhibition. The association will take special care to maintain and protect the submissions. The association will not be responsible for compensation in the event of accidental loss. The submissions will be rotated for exhibition in Nanjing, Shanghai, and other places. After the close of the exhibition, they will be returned to the owner. Submissions cannot be withdrawn at will during the exhibition period. Submissions from all regions must be sent by printed matter registration before the end of March to the receiving office of the National Photography Exhibition at the International Society in Nanjing and Shanghai (26 Shibanqiao Road, Nanjing General Office) (14 Dingxing Road, Parker Road, Shanghai Branch). Late submissions will not be accepted. During the exhibition, for publicity purposes, all submissions may be reprinted in various books, newspapers, and magazines.

The tuberculosis mortality rate in Denmark is very safe. The rate in cities is 6.3 per 10,000 people, and the rate for the entire country is 7.5. Statistics for the whole of Russia are inconsistent. Currently, the tuberculosis mortality rate among the Russian ethnic group is higher than that of other ethnic groups within the Soviet Union. It is lower in eastern Siberia. Tuberculosis statistics in North America show that the peak in mortality is closely related to population density. At the beginning of this century, tuberculosis mortality ranked first among all causes of death in the United States, but now it has fallen to sixth place. It is even lower in Michigan than in the southern states. In Cleveland, in 1930, there were only 8.3 deaths per 10,000 residents. The reduction in mortality is not as great among people of color. The tuberculosis mortality rate in Mexico has also decreased in recent years. Tuberculosis mortality rates in South American countries such as Argentina and Brazil are high due to poor public health. In the Philippines, the tuberculosis mortality rate was 30.55 per 10,000 residents in 1930. The situation in Japan and China is similar to the above-mentioned regions, but it should be noted that mortality rates vary within each region. Tuberculosis is less common in northern and western China, while tuberculosis transmission is more common in central and southern China. In the last hundred years, most black people have migrated to the Americas and become part of the Sklaraki race. Statistics for the United States of America show that the mortality rate is 7.2 per 10,000 residents for whites and 23.2 for people of color, which is more than three times higher than that of whites. Tuberculosis specialists call this racial susceptibility. Statistics for 45 major cities in the United States show that the mortality rate has decreased significantly, averaging 8.23 per 10,000 people. Chicago has only 6.6. However, the mortality rate for black people is still ten percent. The reasons for these racial differences are difficult to resolve, but the general situation is, of course, also related. The situation with tuberculosis in "rural areas" is demonstrated by a report from the League of Nations' International Health Bureau, which shows the highest tuberculosis mortality rates in less developed agricultural areas. However, most scholars still believe that tuberculosis transmission is, on average, lower in rural areas. It is most noteworthy that people who move from rural areas to cities are more likely to experience severe disease changes within the first two years, especially young people. The relationship between tuberculosis mortality and "age," according to German statistics, is almost equal between the sexes between the ages of 30 and 70. Between the ages of 5 and 30, the rate is higher for women than for men. The mortality rate for school-age children has also been gradually declining. It is important to note that new infections are more common among girls than boys in schools, which also proves that tuberculosis transmission does not occur very early in childhood, but at a later age. The most important reasons for reducing transmission are improvements in school facilities and immediate isolation after the discovery of the disease. Recent studies on the transmission of tuberculosis among school-age children show that most infections occur within the family, with very few cases occurring in schools. In large-scale examinations, tuberculosis is found in one to three percent of university students, and there is also a tendency for active tuberculosis to increase. Regarding the relationship between occupation and tuberculosis, nurses and doctors are, of course, the most susceptible to infection. This particular occupation is more dangerous than others. Those who inhale large amounts of dust, such as shoemakers and sewers, also have higher infection rates. In northern Italy, it was found that 1 percent of residents over the age of 60 with tuberculosis have open tuberculosis. According to German statistics on open tuberculosis, the number should be multiplied by at least three times the annual mortality statistics. If the 1932 German mortality rate of 7.5 per 100,000 people is multiplied by three, it becomes 22.5, which, based on the country's population, is 146,250 people. The average life expectancy of these patients with open tuberculosis is three years, which is a major cause of transmission to family members. The case of "tuberculosis among couples" is also noteworthy. Male patients often infect their healthy wives, because women often have pregnancy and childbirth, or because they try their best to take care of their husbands, which makes them more susceptible to infection. However, tuberculosis among couples is not as terrible as one might imagine, because married people are mostly past the most dangerous period of susceptibility. Recent world literature and statistics show that countries such as England and the United States have achieved very satisfactory results in tuberculosis prevention, with only 7 or 8 deaths per 10,000 people. France and Switzerland have also made great efforts in tuberculosis prevention, but still have higher mortality rates. In short, tuberculosis transmission is still very severe in various countries. Without adequate financial resources, the success of tuberculosis prevention will be difficult. What we must pay urgent attention to in the future is the organization methods of "unemployment insurance" and "health insurance," which are the greatest driving forces for reducing tuberculosis mortality. Looking at the success of tuberculosis prevention in various countries, this is the only way. Recent Overview of Tuberculosis in Various Countries; Lecture by Dr. Ding Huikang 120

Dr. Ding Huikang, director of the Hongqiao Sanatorium in Shanghai, went to Europe years ago to investigate the latest tuberculosis prevention facilities in various countries and returned to China last month, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, at the invitation of the Shiqiu Chinese Student Association, he gave a lecture at the association on "Recent Overview of Tuberculosis in Various Countries." More than 200 people attended, including members of the association, professors and students from various universities in Shanghai. First, Chairman Zhu Shaoping gave a speech, followed by a lecture by Dr. Ding, which mainly said that if we want to prevent the occurrence of a disease, we must not only study the causes, but also pay attention to the disease's growth, decline, historical changes, and its relationship to human geography. In the industrial areas of European countries, due to the gradual improvement of their sanitation facilities, the tuberculosis mortality rate has also gradually decreased. In Germany, the number of deaths per 10,000 residents has decreased from 12 to 7.5. The reason is due to the public insurance organization and the progress of public health. In the most recent century, Norway maintained the lowest number of tuberculosis mortality rates, with Denmark being the lowest in 1910, and the Netherlands having a lower mortality rate than Norway in 1920. After the war, the statistics for Switzerland, England, Sweden, and Germany showed that their mortality rates all decreased. Recent observations show that Germany has a lower tuberculosis mortality rate than other countries, making it the country with the least tuberculosis mortality rate in Europe and the world. Tuberculosis calculations in Canada are very high, with a mortality rate seven and a half times higher than that of other people. In British Australia, the age of tuberculosis transmission is very late. The tuberculosis situation in India is relatively poor, with a very high mortality rate, with 30 deaths per 10,000 people per year. In Italy, due to the density of residents in cities, the lack of squares and gardens, and the smallness of most workshops, there are major causes of tuberculosis transmission. In Northern European countries such as the Netherlands, the number of annual deaths is less than the number of beds in the country's hospitals. In countries such as England, the United States, and Germany, the number of deaths and the number of hospital beds are almost the same. In France, there are two deaths for every hospital bed. In Italy, there are five deaths for every hospital bed. The number of deaths has been decreasing since 1925, until 1930, tuberculosis statistics have decreased by 32%. The government that implemented tuberculosis prevention work in Italy was the fascist government, which implemented mandatory tuberculosis insurance, and the results were very good. The tuberculosis mortality rate in France is also relatively high. Although the organization of the current "tuberculosis prevention network" is very complete, the results are not very satisfactory. In general, the tuberculosis mortality rate in Europe is the highest in France. The mortality rate in Belgium is very safe. In Switzerland, the tuberculosis mortality rate has not decreased much compared to its total mortality rate, and is higher than that of other European countries such as Austria, Hungary, Ireland, and Finland. The age of death is mostly during childhood. The tuberculosis mortality rates in Southern European countries such as Romania and Greece are high. The climate in Hungary is harsh, and the construction of houses is very difficult, so tuberculosis in that country can be called a residential disease. The tuberculosis mortality rate in Northern Europe is relatively safe, such as in Denmark, Norway, and Sweden. The tuberculosis mortality rate in Norway has also decreased. Xu Xueseng Doused with Acid; Knew a Secret; Wealthy Man Zhu Murdered Beloved Concubine; To Prevent Leakage, Hired Criminals to Commit the Crime 121

Xu Xueseng, a native of Songjiang and former magistrate of a certain county in Gansu, is 45 years old and lives at 9 Dongmingde Lane, Marang Road, French Concession. On the afternoon of the 6th of last month, at 5 p.m., he went to the Xinxin Bathhouse on Baer Road with his friends Xiao Ronggen and Fu, and two others. At about 8 p.m., as he walked out and passed in front of 26 Wangzhi Road, from east to west, a thug suddenly drove a motorcar, approaching from west to east. He suddenly poured a glass bottle full of corrosive acid on Xu's face. Xu was unable to dodge in time, and his face was burned and he fell to the ground. The perpetrator, seeing that his goal had been achieved, tried to escape. Seeing this, Xu's friends immediately stepped forward to restrain the perpetrator, but the perpetrator resisted and tried to escape. Accidentally, he spilled the remaining acid in the bottle on his own face, and was also injured. At this point, he surrendered. Later, detectives Zhou Bingcheng and Zuo Qihong arrived and sent the injured to the hospital for treatment. It is said that Xu Xueseng was seriously injured, and his right eye may be blinded. The perpetrator's injuries were minor, and after bandaging by a Western doctor, he was taken to the police station. The perpetrator confessed that his name was Gao Jinsheng, 25 years old, from Changshu. He was hired by a fugitive named Hou Laosi to douse Xu with acid. Later, the detectives investigated the case and found that a wealthy man named Zhu from the victim's hometown had murdered a beloved concubine last year. The victim knew about this, and the wealthy man feared that the victim would reveal the secret, so he repeatedly tried to put the victim to death. This tragic scene occurred. However, the victim had heard rumors and was wary, so he always went out in Shanghai with friends. He was still victimized. Yesterday, the police sent Gao to the Second Special Court. The police lawyer requested a postponement, and Chief Wang Tingyi approved a postponement for further trial on the 18th. The defendant's injuries were not healed, and he was sent back to the hospital for treatment.

Amidst Official-Merchant Joint Venture of the Fish Market; Industry Talks About Pros and Cons 125

Guowen News Agency reports that in order to avoid difficulties, the Ministry of Industry's fish market is said to be operated jointly by officials and merchants. According to a reporter's interview with fish merchants familiar with the Shanghai market, the Ministry of Industry's establishment of the fish market was originally a preliminary step towards controlling the national fishing industry. However, if the Shanghai fish market is operated jointly by officials and merchants, the existing large market at 16 Pu will inevitably have to maintain its current status. As a result, 16 Pu will become a branch market in an informal way. Fish vendors will inevitably flock to 16 Pu due to habit, rather than going to Yangshupu. In addition, the inconvenience of transportation to the fish market is a shortcoming. As a result, the transaction of the main market will be taken away, which will defeat the original intention of the government. It is hoped that the authorities can carefully consider this.

Leaf, Aged Twenty-Eight Years, Seeks Confirmation of Biological Mother, Demands Monthly Alimony of Fifty Yuan, Both Sides Present Witnesses to Narrate the Past 127

Madam Ye Chen, a resident of Lane 81, No. 690, Dongxi Huade Road, Hongkou, is the concubine of Hu Sheng, the youngest son of the late Ye Chengzhong, who donated funds for education. In her youth, she was a courtesan, known as Lin Xiaoqing, attracting attention with her beauty. She was favored by Ye Hu Sheng, who redeemed her from prostitution in the 34th year of the Guangxu reign of the Xuantong Qing Dynasty and kept her in a residence on Six Ma Road. The following summer, Madam Chen gave birth. Hu Sheng, because his elders had once said that if a son was born, he would be allowed to live together, but if a daughter was born, she would not be allowed to live in the side room, announced at that time the celebration of having a son, and welcomed Madam Chen back. This has been twenty-eight years. Hu Sheng has passed away for more than three years. Recently, a woman, Ye Yueying, has hired two lawyers, Fan Gang and Ma Leming, to file a lawsuit against Ye Chen in the First Special District Court, claiming that the child born by Chen was actually the plaintiff. Because the elders had insisted that Hu Sheng could not take her as a concubine if she gave birth to a daughter, Chen sent the plaintiff to her aunt Ke Shi's house for foster care after the one-month celebration and sought another boy to be a biological son, so as to avoid condemnation from the family. However, the plaintiff has been abandoned by her parents for twenty-eight years. Therefore, she requests that the court order confirmation that the plaintiff is the defendant's biological daughter and that she be paid alimony of fifty yuan per month. After a preliminary hearing, Judge Luo Chongtai held a hearing yesterday afternoon, summoning witnesses and questioning them separately. However, the defendant, Ye Chen, only hired lawyer E Sen to represent her.

He stated that the defendant is currently in Ningbo and cannot attend. Judge Luo first questioned Zhu Ajin, an old woman from Suzhou who was a witness. According to her testimony, in the first year of Xuantong, she worked as a servant in a small house in Renshou Lane on Six Ma Road rented by Ye Hu Sheng. The plaintiff was indeed born to Chen in June of that year. She initially breastfed her until after the full month, when Chen had to return to the old house with Ye, so she sent the girl to her aunt's house for foster care. Then, Chen's sister-in-law, that is, the plaintiff's aunt Ke Shi, testified that Chen was born on June 25th in the first year of Xuantong. After the plaintiff's one-month celebration, she handed the daughter over to the wet nurse she hired for care, and Chen returned home with Ye Hu Sheng. Not long after, she heard that she had given birth to a boy. According to the witness Fang Guizhang, who was invited by the defendant, Chen married Ye and gave birth to a boy named Lianfu in June of the following year. At that time, I lived in the same house as him, so I knew him very well. The midwife was the German doctor Keli and no daughter was born. The court believed that this case must order the defendant to appear in court for confrontation before it can be clarified, so it ordered a change of date to the afternoon of the 18th of this month to summon the defendant to court for further questioning.

He began an investigation. Coincidentally, No. 51 opposite the tobacco shop was empty. Detective Li contacted the watchman at No. 2259 there. Every night, he would climb to the roof to observe. Sure enough, he saw shadows moving about on the upper floor of Tongshun, working very busily. The detective confirmed the facts, so he, together with anti-drug detectives Wang Rulin and Guo Ruiquan, applied to the First Special Court for a search warrant and went to arrest them at 11:15 AM the day before yesterday. Unexpectedly, they were well-informed and had already moved some important items. The upper floor was also empty. They arrested six suspects downstairs: Chen Zhenqiao from Yong, Wang Gen and Xiao Shui from Chaozhou, Zheng Zhiming and Yao Si from Shantou, and Chen Tong. They confiscated more than 20 scattered items for manufacturing drugs, including a magnetic funnel water tank, scales, and wrapping paper (the paper was still stained with poisonous substances - permission). It was also learned that the Tongshun Tobacco and Paper Shop was opened by Lin Hanqing. Lin's family lives at No. 24, Chengdu Fang, Chengdu Road. The detectives went to Lin's house, but Lin had already fled upon hearing the news. They only found 16 items in the room that were used for making drugs, including glass tubes, soda tablets, and a machine, seals, and account books, which were all taken back to the Chengdu Road Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, recounted the circumstances of the arrest, stating that the main culprit in this case was at large, and that the tobacco and paper shop he opened was actually a fake. He deliberately posted a notice at the door to rent out the remaining rooms upstairs, believing that he could avoid the attention of the police. In reality, the upstairs was used exclusively for manufacturing drugs. Therefore, the police requested that the individuals arrested be detained for a week in order to arrest accomplices, and that the poisonous substances on the wrapping paper be scraped off and sent to the Engineering Bureau's Health Department for testing to determine whether they were morphine. Under questioning, Wang Gen confessed that the morphine manufacturing operation was led by Lin Hanqing, with Jiang Mingsong as his deputy. He used to work on a ship, but now that the ship has been sold, he is temporarily staying with Lin. It has only been ten days. Their work is very secret and they do not let me know. The others all tried to shirk responsibility and refused to tell the truth. Judge Wu Zehan verified the confessions and ordered that Chen Zhenqiao and the other six be detained for seven days for further questioning.

Automobile Turned off Lights and Honked Horn; Investigation Revealed Smuggling of Foreign Silk; Yesterday, the Road Police Section Handled the Case Together 131

At about 7:00 PM the night before last (the 6th), Yin Qi, an outside affairs officer from the Su Song Third Police Section of the Shanghai North Station, was inspecting the post at the intersection of Wangjiazhaizhai Road and Huiwen Road behind the station when he suddenly saw a car speeding towards him, stopping at the street corner, turning off the lights, and honking the horn frequently. After a while, he saw shadowy figures carrying large packages resembling bedding onto the car from the lane. A burly man was directing back and forth, jumping into the car, and ordering it to drive quickly. The officer, being alert and quick-witted, suspected theft and immediately stopped them. Unexpectedly, the man stepped forward and claimed his surname was Liu, and that the packages in the car were all smuggled foreign silk, purchased in Tianjin, and brought to Shanghai by the Huping train. He pleaded for them to be released. The other men helping with the transportation scattered like startled birds. The officer believed that carrying large packages at night was similar to theft, and even if it was smuggled foreign silk, it was still a violation of regulations. He escorted the car and the people and goods to the section for handling. After an interrogation, yesterday morning (the 7th), he telegraphed the Jianghai Customs to send personnel to take custody of them and handle the case according to law. It is said that a total of thirty-five packages of smuggled foreign silk were seized, worth about seven hundred yuan.

Circular Order to Shanghai Maritime Circles: Commercial Vessels Not Allowed to Enter Magong Port; Japan Prohibits Commercial Ships from Entering; Additional Ports Opened Between Kaohsiung and Pingtung 138

Two years ago, a ship of the Sanbei Company encountered a storm on the waters of Taiwan and entered Magong Port for shelter. It was detained by the Japanese naval authorities, and it was only after repeated negotiations that it was released. Last year, several typhoons occurred in the South China Sea, and many Chinese and foreign ships that sought refuge in Magong Port were also detained by the Japanese navy. The port has been designated as a Japanese military fortress area, and all foreign commercial ships are absolutely prohibited from entering. Recently, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, in document Guo Zi No. 1751, notified the Ministry of Communications, relaying a report from the Consul in Taipei, that the Japanese naval authorities had notified that Magong Port had been designated as a fortress military port, prohibiting Chinese and foreign commercial ships from entering. However, due to the large waves in the waters off Taiwan, foreign ships often enter without permission. Therefore, due to the prohibition of commercial ships from going to Magong, the Japanese authorities have established a general port near Kaohsiung and Pingtung to provide shelter from storms and temporary anchoring in the waters off Taiwan. However, sailing ships are subject to Article 2 of the Tax Regulations of the Taiwan Customs, Imperial Edict No. 52 of the 24th year of Meiji, which stipulates that sailing ships not propelled by horsepower are not subject to the prohibition and may still enter and exit Magong Port as usual. The Ministry of Communications has issued instructions to all shipping merchants in Shanghai, ordering them to inform all ships to take note. From now on, except for sailing ships, our country should not enter Magong Port again.

Fang Lianzu and Japanese National Sell Drugs, Caught in Their Own Net; Japanese Offender Sent to Japanese Consulate for Interrogation 139

At 11:20 PM last night, Wan native Fang Lianzu, accompanied by a Japanese pharmacist named Yakushiji, reported to the Laozha Public Concession Police Station that they had suddenly encountered four bandits near North Sichuan Road and Yunnan Road, who robbed them of 13 yuan in legal tender. They requested an investigation. Detective Yang Dechun and the Western detective questioned Fang and the Japanese separately. Finding many suspicious points, they searched Fang and found 13 packs of heroin and 2.23 yuan in legal tender in his inner pocket, as well as a notebook. The notebook revealed that Fang had sold as many as 1,164 packs of heroin since the 2nd of this month. After detailed questioning, Fang confessed that since the 1st of this month, he, the Japanese Yakushiji Yamada, and three Chinese nationals had organized a heroin selling ring on the upper floor of No. 50 Yunnan Road. Around 10 PM tonight, four people came pretending to be police officers, robbed Yakushiji of 20 yuan in banknotes and three packs of heroin on the table, hence the report. The detectives went to No. 50 Yunnan Road to search, but all the drugs had been hidden, so they found nothing. They detained Yamada and sent him and Yakushiji to the Japanese Consulate for interrogation. Fang was sent to the First Criminal Court of the Special District Court yesterday. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang explained the situation, stating that the case still needed investigation and requesting a postponement. Fang Lianzu confessed to running a drug selling business with the Japanese, admitting it without reservation. The court asked whether the business was based on profit-sharing or wages. Fang replied that the Japanese paid him a daily wage of 0.6 yuan. Judge Qian Hongye noted that this kind of business was extremely harmful and should be severely punished. As further investigation was needed, he ordered Fang to be detained and the hearing postponed.

Sports News

Portugal Loses 2-3; Chinese Team Retains the Wanguo Cup; Key Portuguese Players Corazza and Costan Absent; Chinese Team's Victory is a Natural Outcome 148

The Shanghai Wanguo (International) Football Championship has once again been won by the Chinese team. Yesterday's final against Portugal at Yiyuan attracted 8-9,000 spectators. Portugal was missing two key players, Corazza and Costan. Even though Remédi made a comeback, acting as a strong defender, he could not shake the Chinese team's momentum and undermine their chance at the championship. Seeing the Portuguese team's weak lineup, most people predicted that the Chinese team would win even before the match began. As a result, the Chinese team completed their championship with a score of 3-1. Recalling last year's final, also between China and Portugal, the Chinese team won 3-2, which is quite a coincidence. The Portuguese team had great confidence this season, fully expecting to win the championship, but their wish was not fulfilled. Unfortunately, as the competition approached, key players such as Corazza and Costan were unable to play due to injuries, resulting in failure.

Portuguese Coordination Acceptable

The Portuguese team started by using new players and fought hard at the beginning, showing great momentum, but gradually weakened due to a lack of experience and failed to maintain the glory of opening the scoring. The team's coordination was good, but their kicking power was weak. They mainly used small passes to attack the center, and there was little activity on the wings, which was not ideal. Therefore, it was difficult for them to break through the Chinese defense line. The goalkeeper was able to use correct judgment to deal with incoming balls and made many saves. Remédi was the soul of the defense line. He was calm and composed, responding to the Chinese forwards' fierce attacks and making a great contribution. The rest of the team also did their best and remained unremitting.

Chinese Team's Momentum Not Smooth

The Chinese team's victory was inevitable, but their performance was not particularly outstanding. The forwards were sometimes confused and unable to cooperate with each other. The front and back lines were separated, and the defense could not support the offense, resulting in an isolated forward line. Sun Jinshun's adjustments in the second half changed the situation. The team's lack of coordination prevented each player from fully displaying their skills. With the weak power of the enemy's forwards, it was not easy to penetrate deep into dangerous areas. The result of 3-2 did not really reflect the tension of the game.

Gonçalves Opens the Scoring

In the starting lineup, Portugal launched a spirited attack on the Chinese team's position with great momentum. Jiang Shanjing made several saves, protecting Ting Shan. Chen Zhenhe launched an attack from the border, Remédi waited patiently, calmly seizing the ball, and Yi Chen advanced in the center, picking the ball forward. Zhong Yongshen rushed forward to catch the ball but was intercepted by the Portuguese goalkeeper. The Chinese team made several attacks, but Remédi defused the danger with steady steps. The Portuguese army seized the opportunity to attack, advancing from the center and reaching the Chinese goal, creating a tense situation. The Chinese team made a slight negligence, and Portuguese left inside forward Gonçalves stole a shot and opened the scoring, only ten minutes after the start of the game.

Sun Jinshun Scores with a Header

With the win and loss decided, the audience's emotions were intense. Because the Chinese team's attack was unfavorable and they suffered a counterattack from the enemy, they tried to recover their lost ground. The troops on the left moved forward. Sun Jinshun was the first to kick, firing a shot, the enemy goalkeeper was shocked, unfortunately, the ball bounced back from the goal post, Yi Chen spurred his horse, continuing to besiege the city, although he succeeded, he was offside, at this time the Chinese team's momentum was very strong, but the enemy's camp was heavily guarded, unable to enter it, 25 minutes later, Chen Zhenhe dribbled the ball in, to the edge of the penalty area, the enemy was penalized for stealing the ball, Gu Dangxiong kicked, the landing point was excellent, the goalkeeper rushed out to hit the ball, Lao Sun greeted it with his head, opening the scoring, creating a tie.

Li Yichen Also Scores

After that, the two sides stalemate again, you come and go, no chance, the situation gradually became dull again, the Chinese team's front and back were separated, unable to communicate, Portugal's short pass, also lost its effectiveness, the wings were weak, with no progress, 42 minutes, Yichen scored another goal, the Chinese team then turned defeat into victory, stimulating the Portuguese team to counterattack, pouncing on the Chinese fortress, getting a corner kick opportunity, just as it was about to be kicked, the first half ended, after a break, the Chinese team made significant progress in communication in the second half, while Portugal was determined to resist, the ball situation was often exciting,

Penalty Decides the Game

Portugal still adopted the strategy of preemptive strike, attacking the Chinese team, the forward and guard called into one breath, able to activity, how could the Chinese team show weakness, Lao Sun made consecutive supply, so that the contact was quite successful, both sides missed a lot of food opportunities, at 10 minutes, Jia Youliang in the corner position, passed the ball in front of the enemy team's goal, the kicking power was very accurate, Yi Chen shot hard, the ball touched Gonçalves's hand, the penalty was a penalty kick, Sun Jinshun kicked, sent the ball into the corner, the opponent could not save it, the Chinese team then took the advantage with three to one, the game was decided from then on,

Victor Secretly Releases a Cold Arrow

Chen Zhenhe relied on his strong physique, sprinting very fast, and repeatedly stirred up trouble, making the enemy army uneasy, Yongshen Youliang, seemed to have a little more barrier, unable to receive the wonderful effect, but in general, the Chinese stood on the best battle line, making Portugal unable to resist, lacking the strength to attack, unfortunately, there were very few scoring opportunities, Zhenhe Yichen Jinshun repeatedly launched high balls, so that the record could not be increased again, stalemate for half an hour, the Portuguese team suddenly stood out, out of the blue, Victor secretly released a cold arrow, Zhang Rongcai's line of sight was blocked, the ball bounced off his body into the goal, inadvertently losing a goal, the result became three to two,

Shanghai's 20,000-Meter Long-Distance Race Starts at 9 AM This Morning in Front of Fudan University; 154 People Participate in the Open Group, 5 in the Exhibition Group; 22 Quota Places Totaled; Rich Prizes 149

The Shanghai Education Bureau's 4th 20,000-meter long-distance race will be held in the city center at 9 AM today. A total of 154 athletes are participating in the open group and five in the exhibition group. The open group has a quota of 15%, totaling 22 athletes. All athletes must arrive for roll call before 8:30 AM. The Education Bureau has prepared special vehicles for all referees and Boy Scouts, which will pick them up at the Dongya Institute of Physical Education and Laoximen at 7:30 AM, and at the Municipal First Sports Ground at 7 AM. Details are as follows:

Competition Rules. During the competition, athletes should advance entirely according to the route set by the association. If an athlete runs the wrong route, he should return to the original wrong place and run again. They must not step onto the sidewalk, ask for help, or obstruct other athletes from moving forward. Also, each athlete should notify their caregivers to wait at the rest stops. They are not allowed to ride bicycles alongside the athletes during the competition, disturbing order. The roll call point is between Fudan University and Southeast Women's Physical Education School.

Specified Route. Start in front of the Fudan University gate on Xiangyin Road, go through Huangxing Road, Kongjiang Road, Mayushan Road, Guanyintang Road, Jungong Road, Puxi Road, Zhayin Road, Minqing Road, Zigang Road, Guoguang Road, Zhengtong Road, Songhu Road, Zhengtong Road, Guohe Road, Fuxi Inner Road, to the front of the Municipal Government, totaling 20,000 meters. Each distance is marked with Arabic numerals from 1 to 10, dividing the entire journey into ten stages, with each stage being a distance of 2,000 meters.

Statistics on Participants. This year's participants have restricted qualifications, so long-distance running experts are listed as exhibitions. This year's participants increased by two-thirds compared to last year. There were 101 participants last year and 154 this year. Analyzing the professions of the participants, last year there were 51 merchants, 16 workers, 15 students, 12 military police, and 7 others. This year there are 62 merchants, 17 workers, 28 students, 27 military police, 1 doctor, and 24 others. This year, 15%, or 22 people, will be selected according to regulations. Those who reach the finish line will be given medals to encourage them.

Rich Prizes. This year's prizes are very rich. The following is a list of cash and silver shields donated by honorary consultants from all walks of life and produced by the Long-Distance Running and Race Walking Association: Beisongsun, 20 yuan; Ye Zhuotang, 20 yuan; Chen Xing, 20 yuan; Zhou Zongliang, 20 yuan; Chen Zixin, 10 yuan; He Bingsong, 10 yuan; Xu Jiqian, 10 yuan; Li Shizeng, 10 yuan; Hu Zutong, 10 yuan; Li Zhaosai, 10 yuan; Cai Jingjun, 10 yuan; Weng Zhilong, 10 yuan; Jun Yi, 5 yuan; Li Denghui, 5 yuan; Tong Xingbai, 4 yuan; Li Dachao, 2 yuan; Law School, 1 yuan. Prizes: Kong Yongzhi, a special silver shield; Hu Yuntang and Shou Min, a genuine silver cup; Lin Yibo, a genuine silver bowl; Zai Boqi, two silver shields; Wu Xingya, a silver shield; Wu Yunzhai, two silver shields; Wu Kaixian, two silver shields; Fan Jimei, two silver shields; Zheng Tonghe, a silver ding (tripod); Huang Bohui, a silver shield; Li Tingan, two silver shields; Wang Yansong, two silver shields; Wang., a small horizontal scroll painting; Lu Jingshi, a silver mirror frame; Huang Zaoxiong, a silver shield.

Jiang Kanghu's Lecture Today 163

Since Dr. Jiang Kanghu started lecturing on Sinology, the number of Chinese and foreign listeners has been very enthusiastic. The first and second lectures were held on February 23rd and March 1st respectively, with a total of no less than a thousand Chinese and foreign listeners. It is learned that today is the date of the third lecture, starting at 3:00 PM at the Grand Lecture Hall on the fourth floor of the Xin Xin Company on Nanjing Road. The topic is the third section of Part A of the Introduction to Chinese Culture, namely "The Xia, Shang, Zhou, and Spring and Autumn Periods of the Feudal Era—China's First Unification and Expansion." The content is roughly: "The founding of the Xia Dynasty by Da Yu and the exile of his descendants, the first military revolution in China, the founding of the Shang Dynasty by Cheng Tang and the destruction of Jie, the founding of the Zhou Dynasty by King Wen and King Wu, the longest dynasty in Chinese history (800 years), the prosperity of King Wen's administration and military achievements, and the people of the Spring and Autumn Period—the three fundamental systems of the Three Dynasties' culture." The lecture will be given in Mandarin at 3:00 PM and in English at 4:00 PM. It will also be broadcast by Xin Xin Radio (frequency 780).
