Little Boy 166

— Zheng Xiaoxie

A particularly early, light dinner was decided upon, followed by another round of hair-wiping and hand-washing: then this group eagerly looked forward to the arrival of the guests. However, only close relatives were invited; because these small amusements were purely family-style. Later, everyone arrived; Mr. and Mrs. Ma, Siliu and Meg's mother, although she wore mourning clothes, and a small widow's hat surrounded her quiet face, but she was still so gentle and lovely. Aunt Tandi and Uncle Amy, along with their daughter, who is now even more like a fairy, wearing a sky-blue dress, carrying a large bouquet of fruit flowers, which she distributed to the children, inserting them into the buttonholes on their clothes, making them feel particularly exquisite and beautiful. Only one unfamiliar face appeared, Aunt Tandi led this unnamed person to Mr. and Mrs. Pei, and said:

"This is Mr. Hader: he is here to hear about Don playing cards; I boldly led him here, he can see how much this child has progressed."

Mr. and Mrs. Pei beckoned, he was very happy, because of [Don]'s sake, it was still remembered that this child, and he was naturally happy in his heart. However, after a few minutes of conversation, they had a feeling of regret for not having met Mr. Ha sooner, because they found him to be such a cheerful, sincere, and interesting person. When the son saw the light on his friend's face, it was already a pleasant thing: even more pleasant was seeing Mr. Sha's surprise when he saw the progress in Don's appearance and manners; but the most pleasant thing was seeing two people sitting in the corner of the room, deeply talking about topics that they both found interesting, comparing their views, and each telling about their outdoor life in the summer, forgetting the differences in their ages, cultivation, and status.

March 8th Women's Day Special Issue

Our Advocacy 167

— Jin Guangmei

At a time when the national crisis is becoming increasingly serious and the imperialist enemies are intensifying their aggression against China, the commemoration of the March 8th International Working Women's Liberation Day makes us feel that the responsibility of the women's circles in China is even greater, and the significance of the joint commemoration is even more profound!

We are very clear and understand that the current Chinese women's circles demand true liberation, and to obtain true freedom, independence, and equality, we must transform the current social and economic system, and first strive for the success of our national liberation movement!

The position of our country and the environment of our nation are different from all other capitalist countries and all colonies. Our country is a semi-colonial country, and our nation is under the encroachment and oppression of white and red imperialists. Therefore, the responsibility we bear is even greater than that of women in all other countries!

Therefore, we believe that our current urgent task! Should be to take active action against imperialism and feudal remnants as a means to strive for the complete victory of our national liberation movement, to rescue China from the dangerous semi-colonial status, and thereby transform the current social and economic system, and achieve the complete liberation, independence, and equality of our women's circles.

Because of the profound and significant meaning of March 8th Women's Day for Chinese women in this extraordinary period, we have decided to abandon all commemorative forms for this March 8th, and only deeply remember the importance of our responsibility, grasp our confidence, and earnestly implement our work route!

The Meaning of Commemorating March 8th 168

— Cai Jinying

March 8th has a history of more than twenty years. We only recognized its significance after the Northern Expedition. Therefore, gatherings are held and celebrations are held everywhere every year on this day. But when we are commemorating this March 8th in this time of internal and external troubles and national crisis, we naturally have many feelings when we look back and forth!

Our celebration of it is to commemorate past achievements, grasp the current path, and work hard to create future undertakings. Therefore, when we gather to celebrate in high spirits, our hearts are full of enthusiasm, and we expect the public to seek women's happiness. Our commemoration is definitely not a meeting or speech. We should recognize our surroundings, observe the future of women's destiny, and give new strength and new stimulation to the women in deep water and fire, the women who are still not liberated, after this March 8th, to find a bright way out for them. This is the meaning of our commemoration of March 8th.

Superfluous Words on March 8th 169

— Wu Daiyi

Time flies, and "March 8th" is here again. The editor of the "Women's Special Issue" wants to add a word to commemorate the grand festival. The meaning of March 8th has been recorded in detail by previous people. I am not good at writing, so what can I add? But I have been unable to refuse, so I will offer a word reluctantly.

Since "March 8th" began in 1909 until today, the weather has changed twenty-seven times. It has also been introduced to China for nearly ten years. However, our women are still as ignorant as before, the women's movement is still as sluggish as before, and the liberation of women is still as empty as before. How can we not sigh at this grand festival! Recently, the national crisis has deepened and the disaster is imminent. The past cannot be undone, but the future can still be pursued. Our women must reverse the past and invigorate their spirits, be down-to-earth, be aware of the heavy burden, and fulfill their responsibility to help each other. Ms. Zhang Mojun encouraged us with "Return our rivers and mountains and revive our national customs." I am not smart, but I am willing to follow her lead.

Women in the National Salvation Movement 170

— Yan Zhenyu

—Written for March 8th Women's Day—

1936. In this extraordinary period full of crises and imminent dangers, the women of China, no, the oppressed women of the whole world have reached the stage of survival or death. There are clearly only two paths in front of us: one is to fight for survival; the other is to submit to slavery. There is no need for me to explain in detail which way to go. Any sensible woman can make her own choice. Therefore, I think that the women of China, who are in the eve of this storm, should not be able to do anything by just making a declaration and shouting a few slogans on the day of any commemoration meeting. We should recognize our goals, nest our strength, fight for national survival, and shed blood for the freedom and equality of oppressed women all over the world. Only in this way is our proper way out, our current urgent work, and our undeniable task.

Everyone knows that the current world situation is clearly forming two major camps: the oppressors and the oppressed. The oppressive imperialists, because of overproduction, the economy is gradually concentrated in the hands of capitalists, they have to find ways to develop outwards and expand their colonies as a source of absorbing the economy to consolidate their own foundations. Therefore, the imperialists do not hesitate to spend huge sums of money to expand their military preparations and actively develop their colonies to reduce the crisis in their own countries. On the one hand, they want to use the glory of foreign wars to deceive the people, numb the people, and drive the people to the battlefield to die. This is a fact that cannot be denied by the current capitalist imperialists. And the oppressed small and weak nations, seeing the fall of their homeland, fearing the increasing depletion of the national economy, and the difficulty of making a living, naturally united into a united battle line to make a desperate counterattack against the oppressors.

Since the world is an unstable world, and China is a part of the world, it is certainly no exception. Moreover, China is currently under the oppression of a strong enemy and has reached a point of intolerable pain. If we are willing to survive. Then the inevitable path is "resistance." If you are willing to prepare to be a slave, then the inevitable path is "submission." However, I think that except for those who are completely bloodless, no one will want to see China, which has a history of thousands of years, vast land, and abundant resources, being taken by a strong enemy without saving it, and no one will bear to see our compatriots being slaughtered without helping. We are at this critical moment of national survival, and everyone should understand the ancient teaching of "if the skin is gone, what will the hair attach to," and everyone should stand united under the banner of resisting the enemy and fight to the death with the invaders. Therefore, the national salvation movement is the urgent task of the people of the whole country and the work of the people of the whole country who desire to survive. However, there are many ways to save the country, and if there is no unified goal and route, it is easy to fall into divergent and ununified paths. We should stand under the government's command to resist the enemy and continue to struggle with the strong enemy. We must achieve the goal of national liberation before we stop.

That being said, the knowledge of Chinese women is not as widespread as that of men. Many of the work that men can do cannot be compared with men because of women's knowledge and physique. Therefore, I think that in the future, the Chinese women's circles should strengthen their physical fitness and eliminate their weak habits for the national salvation movement. We know that China's most humiliating nickname in the world is the title of "sick man of East Asia." Although this refers to the whole of China, the number of women who are physically unhealthy and weak is indeed higher than that of men. To save China, the first important thing is to exercise our bodies. If the body is not healthy, all methods and claims are in vain.

Secondly, I think that women should resolutely abandon luxury decorations. In recent years, we have been shouting about the bankruptcy of the rural economy and the collapse of the national economy. However, according to the customs' import reports every year, the consumption of women's decorations has been increasing almost every year. This huge outflow of profit sources can make the national economy increasingly depleted on the one hand, and on the other hand, it can be seen that women are becoming increasingly extravagant. This is something that our women's compatriots cannot ignore. Because of the arrival of extraordinary times, the women of the whole country really do not need this kind of consumables.

More importantly, in this period, the women of the whole country should have wartime preparations and universal rescue organizations. If there is no adequate preparation beforehand, not only will they not be able to support the government, but they will also flee in fear of war, which will further affect the work of resisting the enemy. Therefore, I think that before the war, women should have wartime preparations and universal rescue organizations. On the one hand, they can consolidate the morale of the people in the rear, and on the other hand, they can provide substantial help in the war. Moreover, it is quite appropriate for women to take on such work. Although there are many other responsibilities that women should bear, and of course the work of women in the arrival of extraordinary times is definitely not that simple, I cannot describe it in detail here due to the limited space.

In short, I think that for the women of China who are surrounded by strong neighbors, there is no doubt that only resistance is our true way out.

Random Talk on Women's Day 171

— Ms. Hui Ruo

Women's Day is a memorial day for working women seeking "bread and peace." Middle and upper-class women in our country should feel ashamed of the word "labor," because they are idle all day long. I think that the most blessed and lazy women in the world are none other than women from middle and upper-class families in China! They rely on their fathers at home, their husbands after marriage, and their sons after their husbands die. They live carefree lives all day long. They don't know how high the sky is or how thick the earth is. They don't understand the situation of society, the trends of the world, or the troubles of their fathers and brothers earning money. They only know how to reach out to their fathers or husbands for money to study gorgeous clothes, compete for novelty and win. Besides this, they are jealous. This is how they spend their entire lives. Half of this is also because there is an overabundance of laborers in China, so upper and middle-class families all have servants in droves, or at least an old nanny to order around. Therefore, these housewives, besides trying to win their husbands' favor with smiles, consider giving birth to children their greatest achievement. However, they only know how to give birth, not how to raise them, because as soon as their children are born, they hand them over to wet nurses. Afterward, they don't consider or care at all about the children's diet, warmth, health, or how to provide them with a good education. They don't ask about or hear anything, leaving everything entirely to the servants. They only know how to call friends and go to the theater and play cards, and to find out if their husbands are having affairs. Walking into their homes, you only see chaos and smog. It doesn't look like a family!

Therefore, I can't help but feel sorry for ordinary Chinese men. They are beasts of burden for their wives and children all their lives. When they return home, what family happiness do they enjoy?

However, Chinese men don't need to be pitied. They voluntarily become beasts of burden. They use "lack of talent in a woman is a virtue" or "women should return to the family" as tools to bind and restrain women, not giving them the same education as men, making women ignorant and stupid, turning them into playthings for men. They think that knowledgeable women serving in society are taking away men's positions and robbing them of their jobs (they don't know the reason for the increase in the number of unemployed). So they want to drive women back to the family. Think about how cheap Chinese laborers are. They can work like beasts of burden all day long for four or five yuan a month. How clever are the average wives and grandmothers? Who would be willing to save four or five yuan a month and labor hard themselves? They completely hand over housework to servants and enjoy themselves. But when things are too quiet, people naturally want to move around. Since ordinary men are unwilling to let them serve in society, they are happy to take advantage of this and specialize in eating, drinking, dressing, and playing. In the end, isn't it still men who are making trouble for themselves?

However, I want to advise all my sisters: please don't give up on yourselves. See clearly that China is now at a critical juncture of crisis and survival. As the old saying goes, "Everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world." Since men and women are equal, then women should also strive to be good people and shoulder half the responsibility. Women with knowledge and ability should use it to contribute to society. If their knowledge is lacking or if they have young children and cannot leave the family, then they should manage the household diligently and frugally, assist their husbands and teach their children. If they have spare energy, they should further study advanced knowledge to revitalize China's declining society.

You should know that the rise and fall of a family can be determined by looking at the diligence and frugality of the housewife. Then, to examine the rise and fall of a country, wouldn't it also be necessary to look at the level of knowledge and ability of the women in the country, and their diligence and frugality? As a Chinese woman, living in this period of national crisis, wake up! Don't live in a drunken dream!

Finance in the Past Year 3. Bonds (Continuation 2) 190

— He Bo

The bond market is closely related to the financial market. This is because the financial industry in our country mostly uses public bonds as a platform for capital activities and profit-making. When finance is tight, bonds are sold to recover cash, and the bond market falls. Conversely, when there is surplus capital, bonds are purchased, and the bond market rises. Therefore, the changes in the government bond market can be used to measure the fluctuations in the financial market. Although the bond market's rise and fall are not limited to this, it is obvious that it is manipulated by the financial sector. The domestic government bond market in our country has two locations: Shanghai and Peiping. However, the transactions on the Peiping Stock Exchange often follow Shanghai. Moreover, only the "96 Public Bond" is traded. Therefore, we will only briefly describe the situation of the domestic bond market in Shanghai. The Shanghai domestic bond market prices for the 24th year are listed below. (Note 2)

According to the bond index, from January to March, bond prices rose by 2.43%. By April, they reached the highest peak, averaging 100.03, which was 5.47 higher than the average at the beginning of the year. After May, the financial situation became increasingly tense, and the domestic situation did not improve. At that time, there was a road of inflation, and the market was tightening. People's morale was declining, and the bond market gradually fell. By November, the bond market rose again, stimulated by the Ministry of Finance's monetary policy. In order to understand the various changes, we will further analyze them below.

In January, due to the New Year holiday, there were only seven trading days in the market. The price fluctuations were narrow. The highest index was 97.66, the lowest was 92.66, and the average index was 95.56. In February, except for the 23rd year Customs Treasury bills rising to 81.9 yuan, there were no significant fluctuations. In March, a sudden rise occurred in the middle ten days. This was because under the atmosphere of international loans, both speculation and investment were enthusiastic. The total index rose from 95.06 to 97.99. April and May were generally unchanged. In June, due to extremely tight credit and the tense situation in North China, a sharp drop was triggered. Various bonds fell by one to six yuan. Subsequently, the fluctuations followed the North China issue. Next, the discussion about implementing inflation caused the bond market to plummet. The average index fell by 6.57 compared to the previous month. In August, the inflation rumors passed, and the bond market returned to a peaceful state. The process in September was still consolidating. In October, the situation changed drastically. The Sino-Japanese relations were dangerous due to the war between Italy and Abyssinia. New low prices unseen in recent years were created. In the last ten days, the dispute between Britain and Italy tended towards peace, and monetary reform gradually became apparent. Therefore, by November, the bond market was entirely affected by the Ministry of Finance's new monetary policy, and it rose daily. Minister of Finance Kong also clearly announced that "after the implementation of the new system for eighteen months, the national finance can achieve a balance of payments." (Note 3) Therefore, all bonds trended upwards. It was rare to see the discount rise by nearly 90%. The transaction volume for this month reached 369,999,500 yuan. The total futures transaction volume for the entire month reached over 810 million yuan, which was also unprecedented. (To be continued)

Shen Bao Children's Volunteer Essay Contest

What Kind of Person Will I Be in the Future 191

— Wang Jianming, Qingdao City Chenglu Elementary School

Being a person is the biggest question, and what kind of person to be is the most difficult question to solve. Such a major question is probably impossible for parents and teachers to solve for me. So, I will solve my own problem myself!

The treacherous currents, like raging waves, are running wildly. Generally, ignorant youths, confused all day long, not distinguishing east from west, or black from white, drift with the current, resulting in tens of thousands falling into the boundless sea of suffering. This is all because they have no opinions, no plans, no goals, only focusing on the present, and disregarding the future. So, when the sun sets and they reach the end of their road, they ultimately fail!

Judging from the current trend and the future trend, I am afraid that things are getting worse and it is difficult to reverse. However, no one can shirk their responsibility for social reform. The current society is extremely bad. There are no merchants who are not cunning, no gentry who are not bad, and generally, young people are not corrupt and deteriorated. My opinion is: I cannot save the already overturned tide, but I should be a pillar in the middle of the stream, and I must not go with the flow, drift with the world, and become a corrupt and deteriorated element.

I am willing to be determined to be thrifty, honest, brave, and hardworking. I will not sell foreign goods in business, I will not be afraid of bloodshed when I am a soldier, and I will not be afraid of hardship when I am working. This is my highest principle for being a person in the future. If I do this, even if I cannot improve society, I will never be infected with the bad habits of society and repeat the mistakes of ordinary young people.

Two Model Students 192

— Yan

The families of A and B, with whom I live, each have a child studying at the Central Elementary School here. They are both good students, so they were both selected as model students by the school. Their qualifications for being selected are because: 1. Good academic performance, 2. Good character, 3. Good health, 4. Diligent service, 5. Helpful, 6. Lively, 7. Thrifty, 8. Clean. Children who are eleven or twelve years old can have these eight advantages. The title of "model student" is undoubtedly well-deserved.

Parents should be very happy that their sons are model students at school. But no. The mother of child A told me: "My son likes to eat good things. He cannot stand coarse tea and light meals. If there is no meat in a meal, he will throw bowls and chopsticks and sulk and starve. Thriftiness does not only mean not pursuing beauty in clothing, but also being able to eat coarse food and be content with simple clothes and food. That is true thriftiness. He is also not diligent in service. He is unwilling to do anything at home. If you ask him to sweep the floor or wipe the table once, he is always reluctant and looks unhappy. Two of the eight qualifications are not true. How can he be a model student?"

The father of child B also said: "How can my son's character be considered good? He is afraid to speak and afraid to move at school. He is very restrained. He seems to be a well-behaved student, but he is actually a wooden person. Therefore, the word 'lively' cannot be mentioned. When he sees a stranger, his face turns red and he does not dare to look at him or speak to him. He is also so timid that he does not dare to go out alone. How can this kind of child be called a model student?"

I sympathize very much with what their parents said. I ask, if child A cannot endure hardship, how can he stand in society in the future, even if he has good knowledge? Child B only knows stillness and does not know movement. When he should move, he does not move. When he should speak, he does not speak. When he grows up, he will have no ability to speak or do things. What can he do? Many children are afraid of enduring hardship, and many consider silence and immobility to be good character. Therefore, I wrote this down and asked everyone to check themselves to see if they are like this.

Cerebellum 193

— Rourou

The cerebrum has a descendant related by blood, whose name is cerebellum. It lives very close to the cerebrum. Coming out from the cerebrum's home, passing over a bridge - the pons, you arrive at the cerebellum's home. So they are able to take care of each other.

The cerebellum is very young, and its personality is quite close to that of fish - the lateral line system - so it is not as clever and capable as the cerebrum. Although it was separated from the cerebrum to establish its own household, it cannot wisely create new undertakings, but can only make our human body balanced, stable, and regulate muscles.

However, its aspirations are very upward. Knowing that it has no creative ability, it always tries its best to learn and imitate the actions of its ancestor - the cerebrum. But, after all, because it is too young, although it imitates very well in many places, it never dares to overstep its authority and plunder the cerebrum's proper work. During the day, in front of the cerebrum, it only dares to participate in a little opinion at most. When we sleep at night and the cerebrum rests, it then comes out to represent the cerebrum in handling some trivial matters. This kind of work is most easily seen in summer:

For example: a mosquito is stinging us somewhere. As usual, the local sensory nerve sends a telegram to report to the central brain nerve, but the cerebrum is resting at this time, and the cerebellum receives this telegram. After receiving this telegram, it immediately orders the motor nerve on behalf of the cerebrum: "Quickly go and swat the mosquito away." Our hand unconsciously kills the mosquito, and our cerebrum does not even know it.

However, its age is too small after all, and its childishness is too deep. It often plays jokes with us intentionally or unintentionally. And children are most easily fooled by it. To give an example: when you fall asleep at night and have an urgent need to urinate, the cerebellum receives this report and cannot handle it, so it gives you a dream: you run vaguely to the place where you often urinate during the day, and you urinate happily; and when you wake up, you realize that the "happy urination" is still in bed. This is the reason for the formation of bedwetting in children.

Secondly, it is a money grubber, dreaming of clearly picking up a lot of foreign money, but waking up with empty hands!

These are all jokes that the cerebellum plays on us!

Kaleidoscope of the World 194

— Ren

A Country with a Complex Population - Panama

Children know a lot about the Panama Canal, but they don't know much about the Republic of Panama. Now I will talk about its situation:

Chicks Under the Eagle's Wings

Speaking of the Republic of Panama, it can also be called a weak nation. It was not originally a country, but only a state of Colombia. Later, because the Americans wanted to obtain the Panama Canal rights, they helped it become independent. Then, they used 10 million US dollars to buy five miles on each side of the canal and several islands belonging to Panama. They set up military facilities and sent troops to guard them. The Republic of Panama is almost a protectorate of the United States.

Narrow and Long Like the Character "丁" (Ding)

The Republic of Panama is bordered by the Caribbean Sea to the north and the Pacific Ocean to the south. It is the narrowest country in Central America. If we look at its terrain, doesn't it look like the character "丁" (Ding)? (Viewed from the side) The coastline is winding and there are many harbors.

Very Complex Population

The country has a population of 440,000. The population is very complex. There are Spanish people, Native Americans, black people, Americans, and a few Europeans. There are also many Chinese people. The girl in the picture is a Native American. Her attire is strange and she wears silver rings on her nose.

Close to the Equator, the Weather is Hot

The Republic of Panama is close to the equator and the weather is very hot. The interior is mountainous. The country has many forests. The main products are bananas, chocolate, rubber, mahogany, pearls, and tortoiseshell.

A Startling Past History

The past history of the Republic of Panama is startling. In the 17th century, this place was a place where explorers and pirates ran rampant. Behind the modern city, surrounded by forests, there are still dilapidated old houses, which were destroyed by pirates more than 200 years ago.

Very Easy to Recognize National Flag

The national flag of the Republic of Panama is very easy to recognize. The entire surface is divided into four parts. One quarter is red; one quarter is green; the green square has a white background with a green star; the red square also has a white background with a red star.

The weather is good in spring, fly kites in the suburbs. The wind is strong, the kite is high. The baby's ambition soars to the sky.

— Ying Tian

The Effect of Flower Colors 195

— Yi'an

Flower colors vary in many ways, but they are generally very pleasing to the eye. When the god of spring arrives, the flowers on the earth all compete for beauty and splendor. When we see such a scene, we all rejoice and admire it, thinking that the creator has made these beautiful flowers for human appreciation, and humanity can be said to be extremely happy, and the creator can also be considered to be very thoughtful. However, if we carefully study it, we will know that the colors of all flowers are not entirely for us humans. Their object of competing for beauty and splendor is only insects.

If there were no such thing as insects in the world, all flowers would no longer have any color. Although there is a bright sunny weather, this world will be silently colorless.

Plants need insects as a medium for their pollen to reproduce. Our old saying "bee matchmaker, butterfly messenger" is very suitable for this situation in nature. Plants, because insects help to spread pollen, are no different from merchants who want to sell their goods, so they also use advertisements like merchants. Every flower's bright petals are loudly telling the insects that there are delicious sweet nectar or abundant pollen for them to collect.

There are many kinds of insects, and their appetites are also different, so each different flower color represents a special kind of material. Flowers that need bees to spread their pollen are especially purple or blue-violet.

Yellow and red have little or even no attraction for bees. Recent experiments have shown that bees are colorblind to red: they see red as black, like we see photographic negatives. But ultraviolet light, which cannot be seen by the human eye but can only be sensed by photographic film, can be seen by bees.

Bees sometimes collect from flowers that we call red, but these flowers often have other colors mixed in, rather than being purely red.

Pure red flowers produced in the tropics are pollinated by birds.

Butterflies will collect from many brightly colored flowers. Night-flying moths specialize in collecting white and light-colored flowers.

Convex Lens 196

— Junpeng

Last Sunday, Fuyue was playing with a convex lens in his hand. Dad, while reading the newspaper, said: "Fuyue, what are you playing with?" Fuyue said: "I'm playing with a piece of glass." Dad said again: "This is not called glass, do you know that?" Fuyue thought for a while and said: "This is a convex lens!" Children! Do you know the name of a convex lens? Just because Fuyue's father is a natural science teacher at a small school, the words "convex lens" were already printed on Fuyue's cerebellum.

Fuyue's father put down the newspaper and smiled: "Do you want to see me perform a magic trick?" Fuyue said with a smile: "What magic trick are you going to perform?" Dad walked to Fuyue's side and said: "I'll use the convex lens in your hand to perform a magic trick." Fuyue gave the convex lens to his father. Dad took the convex lens in his hand and walked into the sun, saying: "Fuyue, bring me a piece of paper." After a while, Dad put the convex lens in the sun. Behind the lens, there was an extremely bright point. He put the paper straw on this point. In an instant, he saw strands of smoke gradually rising, and then the paper straw caught fire and burned. Fuyue was surprised and said: "Wow! Wow! That's really strange. How did it burn?" Dad smiled and said: "This is because you know that sunlight travels in parallel. A convex lens has a function. All light rays pass through it and converge at a point behind the lens. In physics, this point is called the 'focal point' - it is also an inverted image of the sun - so the heat at this point is the highest, and the paper straw is naturally easy to burn. In the future, you can understand it in detail in physics, so I don't need to explain it anymore."

Children! Why don't you try it this Sunday?

How to Learn Arithmetic? 197

— Linghu Zhao

Children, what is arithmetic? Simply put, arithmetic is the basic skill for studying science. Usually, the most painful and unhappy subject in school for you is arithmetic, isn't it?

In fact, arithmetic is not difficult. If you are willing to work hard, understand what you read, remember what you understand, and write what you remember, then you will definitely find arithmetic more interesting than other subjects.

To learn arithmetic, the first thing to do is to read the theorems and definitions thoroughly. Use a red pen to mark the places you don't understand and ask your teacher until you have a thorough understanding.

Secondly, do more exercises, because doing exercises is a great way to help you remember. And it is not easy to be proficient without doing a lot of exercises.

When there are complex and difficult-to-solve problems in the exercises that take a lot of time and you still haven't solved them, you can do the next one and put the previous one aside temporarily. When you finish the exercises, redo the previous one. Sometimes you will immediately realize and solve it. This way, you won't waste too much time and your interest will be very strong!

Children, when we learn arithmetic, first, we must understand what we read; second, we must remember what we understand; third, we must write what we remember; and fourth, we must solve what we write. If you can do these four linked steps, no matter how difficult the arithmetic problem is, you will always be able to solve it. You will know when you try it!

The Suspicion of a Flock of Sparrows 198

— Huren

During a drought one year, the grains and grass on the earth withered.

A flock of thin and hungry sparrows gathered together to discuss how to find food. A large sparrow said: "If things continue like this, it will be too bad. Many humans are starving to death. What will we do?"

There was a moment of silence.

Suddenly, a small sparrow said: "I remember there is a granary on East Street. Why don't we go and see if there is any rice to eat?"

Everyone followed it. Sure enough, there was a large granary. The little sparrow was the first to fly in and saw a lot of grain inside. It came out to report to everyone.

Many sparrows flew in and ate their fill. One sparrow suddenly asked: "People have so much grain, why are so many people still starving to death?"

They never solved this problem.

Wang Er took a small kite,

Pasted a small baby,

Held a small hemp rope in his hand,

Went to run on the plain,

A gust of wind blew,

It all relies on the wind to go to the Ninth Heaven,

Never free to run,

The Tale of the Righteous Dog (10) 201

— Xinqing

What did he want to see? Padereshi thought quietly, looking up at Xiao Nanluo with its big, sympathetic eyes.

One day, the gatekeeper happened to be away, and the two large iron gates happened to be half open. It followed Xiao Nanluo in and saw what Xiao Nanluo wanted to see. It turned out to be two extremely large murals on both sides of the choir.

Xiao Nanluo knelt before the two sacred murals, happy as anything. When he saw Padereshi, he quickly stood up and gently pulled it out the door. His face was wet and covered with tears. He looked up at the places covered with cloth in the temple and whispered to Padereshi: - "Padereshi, just because a person is poor and cannot pay, he cannot see those paintings. What a difficult thing that is! I know that the person who painted those paintings would never have refused poor people to see them when he painted them. He must be willing for us to go and see them at any time - to see them every day - I can be sure of that. But they cover these paintings up - cover them in darkness. Those beautiful things! - They have never seen the light of day, and no one's eyes have looked at them, unless rich people come and pay. If I could see them all, I would be satisfied even if I died."

But he could not see those paintings, and Padereshi could not help him, because the price for visiting those sacred paintings in the chapel was very high. To get such a sum of money was as difficult as climbing to the top of the chapel.

They never had any extra money. If they had money, they would have to buy some firewood, put it in the stove to burn, and cook some meat soup in the pot. This was their greatest strength. But the child's heart constantly longed to see those great sacred paintings that were covered up.

In the faint morning light, they hurried through this ancient city. The sun had not yet risen, and people had not yet gotten up. Xiao Nanluo and Padereshi dragged that small cart of milk, delivering it door to door. In the child's dream, he was still seeing the sacred paintings in the chapel. He was cold and hungry, barefoot in wooden shoes. The winter wind blew his thin hair and blew up his thin clothes, but he was still very happy to think that all he saw in his eyes was the majestic face of the Holy Mother Mary, her golden hair draped over her shoulders like waves, and the eternal sunlight shining brightly on her forehead. Xiao Nanluo, a poor child who was illiterate and had no knowledge, and whom people did not pay attention to, knew that he had a natural love for painting.

No one knew. Like such a small child, no one knew.

Only Padereshi, who was often with him, saw him often drawing on stones with chalk, heard him murmuring blessings to the great painters on his straw bed; and saw his little face light up in the slanting sunset or the rosy morning light. Padereshi also felt drops of hot tears falling from his little eyes and falling on his own yellow, furry forehead.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Amateur Weekly

Amateur Ramblings

Dispute Over Telephone Price Increase 202

— As It Is

In the past, Shanghai telephone charges, whether for commercial or residential use, were calculated on a monthly basis without any limit on the number of calls. However, not long ago, the Shanghai Telephone Company suddenly announced new regulations, stipulating that commercial telephone fees would be ten yuan per month for 150 calls, and residential telephone fees would be six yuan and fifty cents per month for 100 calls, with an additional charge of three cents for each call exceeding the limit. After the announcement of these new regulations, most businesses considered it a disguised telephone price increase, which they could not accept in the current economic downturn. Therefore, they formed the "Shanghai Special District Telephone Problem Committee" to negotiate, requesting an increase in the basic number of calls to ease the burden. However, after extensive negotiations by the committee, there were no results; the telephone company's attitude was very firm, and the new regulations were bound to be implemented. Later, the Chinese directors of the Chinese Ratepayers Association put forward four compromise proposals: "1. Revise the per-call tariff schedule recommended by telephone experts as follows: Commercial telephone fees of ten silver dollars per month for 200 calls, and residential telephone fees of six yuan and fifty cents per month for 150 calls; 2. The above revised tariff schedule shall be implemented from April 1, 1936, which is one year after the temporary 11% price increase was implemented (the temporary price increase measure has been in effect since April 1, 1935); 3. After adopting the above revised tariff schedule, if the company's net profit exceeds the permitted 10%, the bureau shall immediately request the company to revise the tariff to immediately reduce telephone fees. If the company's profit is less than 10% after the above revised tariff is implemented, the company shall not request a price increase again within five years from the date of implementation of the tariff; 4. The bureau should ask the company to earnestly economize on operating and maintenance expenses." The Telephone Problem Committee immediately expressed its acceptance of this compromise proposal. However, after discussions between the Chairman of the Municipal Council and the telephone company, the company only agreed to accept the first point of the third article and the fourth article, rejecting all other points. At the same time, for some unknown reason, after the company rejected the compromise proposal of the Chinese directors, the newspapers published a letter from the Chinese Ratepayers Association to the Telephone Problem Committee, stating that many users had "approved and accepted" the company's new regulations; subsequently, the Telephone Problem Committee also expressed its intention to disband in anger in its reply to the Ratepayers Association. Now, the company has officially notified all users that it has decided to implement the new regulations from March 1; under the urging of the citizens, the Telephone Problem Committee has again expressed its willingness to continue its efforts and has scheduled a third joint meeting of various groups on March 10 to decide everything. Therefore, the future of the long-disputed telephone issue will soon be seen.

In fact, the reason why businesses and residents install telephones is undoubtedly for their own practical needs; those who have telephones will certainly use them when necessary, and will never make calls for fun when there is no need. Therefore, the telephone company's so-called new regulations restricting the number of calls for users are obviously not to prevent "waste"; its purpose is clearly for the sake of "profit." Furthermore, according to the actual situation, limiting residential telephone calls to 100 per month may be sufficient, but stipulating 150 calls per month for commercial telephones, averaging five calls per day, is not enough. If a store makes an average of ten telephone calls per day (which is very possible), then according to the company's regulations, it will have to use 150 extra calls per month, calculated at three cents per call, and the store will have to bear an additional telephone fee of four yuan and fifty cents per month. This may not seem like much to the owners of large department stores, but it is difficult for small and medium-sized businesses who are struggling to maintain their businesses to bear this new burden.

Naturally, establishing companies, owning property, and operating all industries and businesses are, to put it bluntly, for the purpose of making profits; the Shanghai Telephone Company undoubtedly wants to earn a little more profit each year, which is not surprising. However, in calculating its own profits, the company should also think about the merchants and citizens who regularly provide them with profits, and consider whether these people can bear new burdens in this economic downturn, and whether they can earn more profit for themselves. We often hear small and medium-sized merchants say that they spend the whole year making money for landlords, water and electricity companies, and telephone companies, and that they are constantly under pressure and never prosper! This is true. Therefore, when many stores announced closures and "big sales" and "great auctions" were advertised on every street, when everyone was really helpless, merchants and ordinary citizens launched a rent reduction campaign to try to alleviate some of the burden; although this campaign has not yet achieved great general success, it has had some partial effects; in fact, rents have been reduced in some places, and some landlords have even voluntarily reduced rents, which is certainly a manifestation of being aware of current affairs. However, under these circumstances, the Shanghai Telephone Company has instead implemented a disguised but actually the most severe telephone price increase, which is really a manifestation of not considering the general merchants and citizens who make money for them at all!

Now, the telephone company's new regulations have begun to be implemented, and general telephone users and even general citizens will certainly continue to oppose them. We hope that the protesters will fight to the end, and we also hope that general citizens will pay attention to all public utilities in this city that are most closely related to our lives, such as water, electricity, and trams. Because these are essential to our daily lives, the people who run these utilities can control us and arbitrarily increase prices at any time. Take this telephone price increase as an example. Why is the telephone company's attitude so firm? On the one hand, it is naturally because, as the Telephone Committee said, they are "relying on the extension of foreign power and holding strong power"; but on the other hand, it is also because telephones are necessary for some families. If these families are unwilling to pay the higher price, the company can remove their telephones, causing them great inconvenience; therefore, they can control these users and forcibly implement the price increase. As for water, electricity, and trams, they are even more necessary for the general public, so their companies can better control the general public, and of course, they are also what we should pay special attention to. The purpose of this attention is to use everyone's strength to monitor the arbitrary price increases of these essential things, in order to excessively exploit us. Everyone should understand that the so-called things that everyone needs

Page 20

are also the things that rely on everyone for their existence. If the price of these things is too high and exceeds the general standard of living, then everyone should deal with it together and not allow its price to be too high. The price of all essential things is naturally determined by the owners of these things on the one hand, but it is also determined by the consumers on the other hand; if the owners' regulations are completely rejected by the consumers, then these regulations will absolutely not be implemented.

A Week of Travel

It's Easier to Climb a Mountain Than to Descend 203

— Liu Yangzhu

I taught at a middle school at the foot of Mount Lu for two years. During those two years, especially during the summer vacations, I received many letters from friends who envied my job location, saying that I must have accumulated good karma in several lifetimes, as I could climb Guling for summer vacation at any time. Little did they know that the reality was far from the truth. Guling did not reject us poor teachers, but economics could limit us. In the summer, the price index in Guling was several times higher than at the foot of the mountain. It was naturally a place for the leisure class to enjoy themselves. In addition, due to the recent revolution and the large number of troops, military expenses were enormous, so it was necessary to transfer educational funds to meet the emergency. As a result, educational funds were sometimes in arrears for as long as half a year. During the school term, we could elect representatives to petition the Education Department for salaries, but once the schools were on vacation, the Education Department knew that no one would come to petition, so they simply ignored it. Therefore, we were particularly poor during the summer vacation, and sometimes even buying rice was a problem, let alone traveling to Guling?

However, we four colleagues did make a determined, arduous journey to Guling. Each of us brought a small amount of money and set off at dawn on a sweltering summer day, walking to Lianhua Cave at about 10 a.m. After resting in a teahouse for a while, eating a few steamed buns, and drinking a bowl of bitter tea, we started walking up the mountain. The mountain road was fifteen li long, but it had neat stone steps, and we all felt that the mountain road was easy to walk on, and that it was easy to climb Guling. After turning several mountain bends, the scenery became more serene and secluded, and the gurgling sound of the springs filled us with a sense of leisure and distance! Halfway up the mountain, there was no trace of heat, the wind moved the bamboo baskets, and the clouds rose beneath our feet, and we couldn't help but shout with joy!

When we were three li away from Guling, it unexpectedly started to rain, and then the wind attacked, the mountains roared, and everything in front of us was dark. My colleague Mr. Cai cried out "Ah!", and the straw hat on his head was blown away. We all felt a little panicked. We had no choice but to walk tremblingly along the mountain cliff. The moss on the stone slabs was particularly slippery. If we lost our footing, it would be a bottomless abyss, and we really didn't know where we would be buried!

None of us had brought rain gear, and our clothes were soaked. Fortunately, we ran into a farmer. We gave him money and asked him to buy us umbrellas. He told us to wait for him in a pavilion. It was truly "seek what is lost from the wilderness." After a short time, he bought us umbrellas, and we mustered our courage and walked up to Guling.

Guling is truly a good place! There are stone paths that are full of poetic charm, with colorful wildflowers blooming everywhere along the paths, and the sound of gurgling streams can be heard everywhere. The buildings are built according to the mountain's terrain, with very few brick walls, mostly built with large stones from the mountain, and the forms and colors of the buildings are rarely the same.

Guling, everything is poetry, everything is painting.

We ran around the streets and nearby mountains for a while, and it was already 3 p.m. The fire of hunger was making us dizzy, and the high prices in Guling were something we had long admired. We found several restaurants, but we didn't dare to go in. Finally, we found a dilapidated noodle shop, assuming that it must not be expensive, so we went in to satisfy our hunger and came out.

After wandering around Guling for a while, a thick fog suddenly rose in the mountains, a vast expanse of white, and even the buildings could not be seen. We wanted to stay in a hotel, but we didn't have any money, so we braced ourselves and went down the mountain. We agreed to take one step at a time, calling out to each other, groping in the fog. The moss on the stone steps, moistened by the rain and fog, was even more slippery. Everyone thought: If we slipped and fell to our deaths, it would be a great injustice! It was truly "walking on thin ice," and after great hardships, we returned to Lianhua Cave, and the tense emotions relaxed a little, but everyone was covered in moss and mud, unrecognizable, and we couldn't help but laugh at each other's embarrassed state.

By the time we got home, it was already 7:30 p.m., and we couldn't move at all when we lay in bed. This trip's experience tells us that "it's easier to climb a mountain than to descend" is an irrefutable theory: because when descending the mountain, one cannot control oneself, and there is the suffering of calling to heaven without answer and calling to earth without response, just as "it's easier to get on stage than to get off," which is the same principle.

Interview with a Celebrity

Mr. You Huaigao, Owner of the Free Farm 204

— Hu Qingyuan

It was an afternoon when the east wind was even more bone-chilling than the north wind. I braved the severe cold and got out of the car at the green bamboo fence gate. After a series of formalities, I was led by a Mr. Pan to meet Mr. You Huaigao, who has dedicated himself to agriculture.

This is a refined guest room, about ten feet square. Although the furnishings inside are not luxurious, they are arranged in an orderly manner. From this, it can be seen that Mr. You is indeed a very serious person in his planning for life. After we exchanged greetings, we began to talk about his business itself.

It is said that although the market has often been in a gloomy state of rain and wind in recent years, the Free Farm has been able to maintain its business without much impact due to proper management. The average daily sales of milk are more than 1,400 pounds in summer and more than 1,800 pounds in winter.

Mr. You is fifty-one years old this year, tall and slender. He was wearing a plain satin silk cotton long robe, with a Western-style shirt underneath and Western-style trousers. With a narrow face, a broad forehead, and a pair of fine tortoiseshell-rimmed glasses, he looked every inch the scholar. After he told me about the current situation of the Free Farm, a look of self-satisfaction shone on his face.

"I heard that Mr. You used to study at Soochow University, but later went to the United States. Why did you change to studying agriculture?"

"This is due to family circumstances. Because my family has a lot of land, most of which is rented to tenant farmers. The miserable lives of those farmers left too bad an impression on me, so I later studied agriculture in the United States, preparing to make some contributions to my country's agriculture after returning home."

"You studied in the United States for many years, right?"

"Well! I went abroad in the first year of Xuantong and returned in the fifth year of the Republic. In those seven years of studying, I was immersed in the study of agriculture every day. Every summer, I had to go to the countryside for internships."

"Such a student's life, according to you, doesn't seem very comfortable!"

"Haha, a student's life is not as comfortable as most people imagine, especially for a student who is diligent in his studies, it is even more bitter. Moreover, because I wanted to graduate early and shorten the period of study, in addition to going to the countryside for internships every summer, I also had to go to the summer school established by Cornell University for supplementary studies; because one summer's course can earn at least six credits, and accumulating four summers can shorten one year."

"Mr. You's motivation for running the Free Farm probably started during his internship in the countryside, right?"

"I didn't think about it at that time. However, I studied rural economics and animal husbandry, so I was particularly interested in the animal husbandry business." He held the teacup tightly with both hands, looking reminiscent.

一This "Free Farm," did you start it after returning home?"

"No!" He paused for a moment, thinking, and said, "Soon after returning home, I and several close friends jointly established the "China Egg Trade Company," using scientific methods to transport eggs for export, but as a result, because the cost was too high, it was difficult to sell, and after more than a year of operation, we lost more than 10,000 yuan and stopped. Later, I wanted to set up a chicken farm, and spent half a year on investigation and design, but as a result, it was also stopped due to various difficulties: First, because egg prices were low and chicken feed was expensive, farmers raised chickens without much expense, and the cost was lower, so it was difficult for chicken farms to compete with them; Second, raising chickens in one place is very easy to cause infectious diseases, while farmers raise chickens scattered in various places, and diseases are rare, so there is no major sacrifice. Although these two businesses both failed one after another, my plan of "three acres of land and freedom" still lingered in my mind. So, in the seventh year of the Republic, I started to attempt to raise dairy cows. I started preparing in the seventh year of the Republic, and I took on all the investigation and design work myself. It took a full year and a half to officially establish it in the ninth year of the Republic. The "freedom" in "Free Farm" comes from my "three acres of land and freedom."

"The start-up capital of the Free Farm is probably very strong, right?"

"No," he said, slightly pausing as if he was afraid of disappointing me, "You don't have to haggle over the amount of money to do a business, but perseverance is very necessary. The Free Farm had only 15,000 yuan in start-up capital, and only three dairy cows, but now, the capital has increased to more than 200,000 yuan."

"In the early days of the business, you probably spent a lot of time planning, right?"

"Well! This really took a lot of careful consideration and selection procedures. The standards for choosing the site for this Free Farm, I first determined five conditions: 1. Convenient transportation, 2. Low rent, 3. Complete facilities, 4. Room for expansion, 5. Lease term of at least twenty years. I asked people everywhere to find a way, and it took a full eight months to find the current site according to my predetermined goals. The annual rent is 200 yuan, and the lease term is tentatively set at fourteen years, later increased to twenty-four years, and the rent has also increased from 200 yuan to 1,000 yuan." The waiter brought a cup of hot milk, and he took a sip and continued with great satisfaction: "After the site was leased, I drew a plan and planned the cowshed, machine room, and writing room, and then applied to the Public Works Department for a permit to start construction." He took another sip of milk, and talked more vigorously as if he was telling a story: "The houses are built of brick, but because of economic constraints, I had to plan everywhere, both economical and beautiful. So, I decided to use white for the walls, green for the doors, and red for the roof; but at that time, foreign red tiles were very expensive, and it was quite difficult to do so financially, so I thought of a way to use the old Chinese tiles and add a kind of red color to make them foreign red tiles. I remember that the famous architect Dr. Lu Yanzhi praised my kind of tiles once."

"How was the business situation when you first started..."

"At that time, there was simply no business to speak of." He interjected before I could finish speaking: "As I just said, there were only three dairy cows when the business started, originally four, costing a total of 3,200 yuan, but one died in transit from Holland; only a little more than 100 pounds of milk were produced every day, and there were only dozens of regular customers. After a year like this, the 15,000 yuan of capital was completely lost, and later I converted my own house into cash and added it to the capital, and continued to operate, and it didn't start to improve until five years of continuous losses. The number of dairy cows increased from three to fifteen, thirty, and now there are a total of ninety; the number of regular customers has also increased from dozens to more than 5,000."

"There must have been a lot of surplus in recent years, right?"

"Since five years after the start of the business, there has been a surplus every year; however, because the organization of the Free Farm is not a company, the annual surplus, except for 4,800 yuan as the annual interest on my 60,000 yuan of capital, is used as a public reserve to prepare for expanding production and purchasing dairy cow machines, etc."

"Since the Free Farm is not a company organization, why bother with such a form?"

"This procedure is not "painting a snake and adding feet." Because although this is not a company organization, there are still some external shares, and the production combination is also collective; if I confuse myself with the farm,

Page 21

then it will not give a good impression to the general working colleagues." As he spoke, he took a notebook from the desk and flipped through it page by page for me to see. "Look, this is the amount of salary that the farm has given me over the years. From 1920 to 1922, I can be said to have been doing business for nothing for these two years, and I didn't take a penny of salary. It wasn't until 1923 that I stipulated 50 yuan per month, and it was increased to 100 yuan in 1925, and then it was increased by 50 yuan every two years, and now it's only 300 yuan. 300 yuan is not too much, right?" He asked me with a smile.

"Considering your contribution to the Free Farm, 300 yuan is naturally not too much! The treatment of the staff here is also not bad, right?"

"I can't say how good it is, but many of the staff and workers here have been working since the beginning, so you can probably guess how good their treatment is from this point." He said very modestly.

"I heard that Mr. You also runs a farm in Suzhou. How is the performance there?"

"Yes, that is run jointly by me and my younger brother, and it has been several years now. The capital is only 10,000 yuan, the farm covers an area of 50 mu, there are more than 30 dairy cows, and the average daily milk production is 500 pounds; he is responsible for managing it there, and the performance is not bad. We also opened a farm in Hangzhou, which is a branch of the Free Farm. The capital is 30,000 yuan, but there are only 15 dairy cows, and the daily milk production is more than 300 pounds."

"In addition to the Dutch breed, are there any other breeds of dairy cows available? Why can't Chinese cows produce milk?"

"The Dutch breed is the best for dairy cows. Although there are dairy cows in California, they are not as productive as Dutch cows. Chinese cows have absolutely no way to produce milk."

"If you cross Dutch cows and Chinese cows to produce calves, can they produce milk?"

"This is a work that requires a lot of effort but yields very little. According to research, at most, the first generation of calves produced by crossing Dutch cows and Chinese cows can produce a small amount of milk, but the rest, such as the second and third generations, have no effect, and by the fourth generation, they will still restore the original characteristics of Chinese cows."

"What is the daily milk production of a Dutch cow?"

"This cannot be generalized, because there are many reasons for this. For example, a Dutch cow can produce 60 pounds of milk per day in its home country, but when it comes to China, it will be reduced to 30 pounds; and when the calves it raises produce milk in the future, it will be as little as a little more than 10 pounds. On average, each of the 90 cows I have here can produce 15 pounds of milk per day." He said a lot, and then used a few machine-made fire　to make statistics and explain to me.

"This is probably due to the soil and water, right?"

"Of course, this is also one of the reasons, but the feeding materials also have something to do with it. Because the food used to feed cows is mostly White-Clover and Alfolfer in foreign countries, these grasses are very nutritious, so the milk production of cows raised in foreign countries is much higher than that of cows raised in China. When I was learning to milk cows in the United States, I saw that they were all feeding cows with white flowers, and almost every farmer with cows had one or two hundred acres of land dedicated to growing that kind of white flowers. This kind of grass contains a lot of nectar when it blooms, and the flowering period is long. In general, farmers not only rely on it to feed cows, but also rely on it to raise honey, but in China, there is not such a large area to supply the grass and feed for cows to eat!"

"Are there farms like this in the United States?"

"The milk business in the United States is very developed, but its organization is very different, and there are even fewer farms like the "Free Farm." Most of the milk sources in the United States come from farmers. Each family produces from 30 pounds to several hundred pounds of milk a day, depending on the number of cows the farmer raises; the milk produced every day has to be sent to a milk collection agency before dawn. After that, the sterilization, bottling, and distribution are all the work of this agency, and the farmer can completely ignore it. It is said that in recent years, this milk business has become even more advanced. The milk collection agency has its own milk collection vehicles, which collect milk along the villages every morning. Farmers only need to write the weight on the milk bucket, and the milk collector will record it for him. This situation can only be done in the United States, but in China, it is not possible to reach that state for a while; this is partly because the organization of Chinese milk companies is different, and partly because the animal husbandry business in rural areas is not yet developed. Therefore, we must improve the milk business in China and pay attention to promoting the animal husbandry business in rural areas at the same time!"

Amateur Coffee Corner

Respecting the Elderly 205

— Zi Man

An old horse knows the way, and an old doctor rarely makes mistakes. These sayings praise "old age." No wonder Guangzhou is holding an elders' gathering and Taiyuan is about to hold a respect-for-the-elderly convention. It shows that "old age" indeed has its respectable value.

"What do you young people know? I've lived for over sixty years and still don't understand, yet you claim to!" It seems that old people must know everything, and young people may not know. Because old people are always "old," they can therefore "rely on their age to act important."

Since "old age" is praiseworthy and respectable, then "youth" naturally has to learn to be more "mature." Even without a beard, they must stroke their chins, cough a few times for no reason, and pace back and forth as if something important is going on.

"I, your old man... you, little brat..." Such empty words sound impressive. Even if you are illiterate and nonsensical, hanging up a sheep's head and selling dog meat, with this "old" sign, who are you afraid of?

However, "old age" that is not handled properly naturally becomes "old and contrary," "old and decrepit," "old and senile," and so on. That is truly the worst kind of "old age." Therefore, "old age" should be made "stronger," which is a remedy for "old age."

Reading a commentary from the "Current Affairs News" on January 10th of last year, "On Respecting the Elderly," it says:

"We believe that the object of respecting the elderly is not respecting their "high age," but respecting their "abundant virtue." Respect those among them who can strive for the benefit of the people, and learn and accept their experiences and lessons in promoting social progress. As for those old, cunning, and slippery scoundrels and white-bearded old thieves like ×××, they have not only become antiques of the times but also obstacles to national rejuvenation...

"...Those remnants of the past who fill society, their spirits and bodies are prematurely aging. In form, they are young and graceful, but their daily lives are no different from those of muddle-headed old people."

Thus, I know that respecting the elderly should be about respecting those who deserve respect. Originally, I thought that old and young were just comparative terms based on age. Everyone is human, and there seems to be no need to look down on or respect them in the crowd.

Seeing those old people who have merely increased their age, not feeling "how easily time passes" and "wasting a lifetime," but instead gloating in their "old age" and taking pride in it, and seeing young people who are strong and energetic not igniting the "fire of youth" but only learning to be "mature," speaking "old words," and burying themselves in ancient books, "thinking all day about how to live a leisurely and carefree life," I can't help but gasp.

Book and Newspaper Review

Review of Zhou Zuoren's "Bitter Tea Essays" 206

— Chen Fu

—Published by Beixin Bookstore, priced at nine corners per volume—

Mr. Zhou Zuoren is a famous essayist in China. His "vernacular Chinese" mixed with many classical Chinese words and phrases has been praised for its "conciseness" and "simplicity." Some master, "wanting to cling to the tip of the bull's horn and defend it for life," even used his articles as a sign for the "quotation style" to resist the new vernacular Chinese. These are all well known. "Bitter Tea Essays" is a collection of his recent essays, including a "preface" and an "epilogue," containing a total of fifty articles of varying lengths. If distinguished by form, these fifty articles can be roughly divided into three categories: first, transcriptions and reflections on reading old books; second, prefaces written for other people's works; and third, general essays and notes. These articles may have been seen by everyone and have already received "positive reviews" in other publications, so there seems to be no need to say more. However, after reading this collection, I feel the need to say a few words, so I picked up my pen to talk about "Bitter Tea Essays."

Although "Bitter Tea Essays" is not a systematic work, but a collection of miscellaneous essays, we can first see the author's view of life in it. In the article "The Lesson of the Frog," the old man Zhitang—Mr. Zhou Zuoren—clearly tells us:

"In fact, it is very unwise to ask the old to follow the young. Among savage tribes, there are two ways to deal with the elderly: one is to kill them and eat them; the other is to have them stay behind in the stockade with the women, when the brave men go out to war. Asking them to run with the young will only result in them panting and their old legs failing, delaying the young's progress. If they are carried along as puppets, they can only scare the village children. In short, neither is the way to "respect the elderly." The elderly have their own time and place. Let them sit in the sun at the door, twisting ropes and making straw sandals, watching over the chicks and ducklings. Those who are elegant can also look at New Year pictures and write Wei-style calligraphy. Don't force children and grandchildren to be filial and hinder their work. That would be good... Those who sell their souls to the devil are said to become people without shadows, and those who dedicate their souls to God are not much different anyway. Those who do not believe in the soul can stand firm, because they have nothing to sell and can stand outside, although scolding is inevitable."

The old man Zhitang is of course old, and the above passage is his defense for the general elderly and also for himself. Based on this defense, he has determined the elderly's view of life that they should not follow the young: he does not want to "sell his soul to the devil" or "dedicate his soul to God," because these are "not much different anyway." Thus, he can only "sit in the sun at the door, twisting ropes and making straw sandals," and drink bitter tea, copy old books, and write doggerel poems; other than that, what national nation, life society...

However, Mr. Zhou's view of life for the elderly does not seem to be solely determined by his old age. This is related to the real country
